----- FILE: /opt/scalp/dp.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# ---------- CONFIG ----------
ROOT="/opt/scalp"
DUMP_DIR="${ROOT}/dump"
mkdir -p "$DUMP_DIR"
TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')"
OUT="${DUMP_DIR}/scalp_full_${TS}.txt"
MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB="${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB:-512}"

# ---------- GIT ENV ----------
[ -f /etc/scalp.env ] && . /etc/scalp.env
: "${GIT_USERNAME:?}"
: "${GIT_TOKEN:?}"
GIT_BRANCH="${GIT_BRANCH:-main}"
GIT_EMAIL_USE="${GIT_EMAIL:-${GIT_USERNAME}@users.noreply.github.com}"
REMOTE_URL="https://${GIT_HOST:-github.com}/${GIT_OWNER:-$GIT_USERNAME}/${GIT_REPO:-Scalp}.git"

# ---------- HEADER ----------
{
  echo "# ===== SCALP PROJECT DUMP ====="
  echo "# $(date -u +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC')"
  echo "# Root: $ROOT"
  echo
  echo "========== TREE =========="
} > "$OUT"

find "$ROOT" -type f \
  -not -path '*/.git/*' -not -path '*/venv/*' \
  -not -path '*/dump/*' -not -path '*/logs/*' \
  -size -"${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB}"k \
  \( -name '*.py' -o -name '*.sh' -o -name '*.conf' -o -name '*.sql' -o -name '*.txt' \) |
  sort | while IFS= read -r f; do
    sz=$(stat -c%s "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    mt=$(stat -c%y "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo unknown)
    printf "%-80s %12s %s\n" "$f" "$sz" "$mt" >> "$OUT"
done

{
  echo
  echo "========== FILE CONTENT =========="
} >> "$OUT"

find "$ROOT" -type f \
  -not -path '*/.git/*' -not -path '*/venv/*' \
  -not -path '*/dump/*' -not -path '*/logs/*' \
  -size -"${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB}"k \
  \( -name '*.py' -o -name '*.sh' -o -name '*.conf' -o -name '*.sql' -o -name '*.txt' \) |
  sort | while IFS= read -r f; do
    echo -e "\n----- FILE: $f -----" >> "$OUT"
    cat "$f" 2>/dev/null >> "$OUT" || true
done

# ---------- DATABASE STRUCTURE (finale complète) ----------
{
  echo
  echo "========== DATABASE STRUCTURE =========="
} >> "$OUT"

for DB_PATH in /opt/scalp/project/data/*.db; do
  [ -s "$DB_PATH" ] || continue
  echo -e "\n----- DATABASE: $DB_PATH -----" >> "$OUT"

  {
    echo "-- TABLES --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" ".tables" 2>/dev/null || echo "(locked or unreadable)"
    echo

    for T in $(sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" ".tables" 2>/dev/null); do
      echo "[TABLE: $T]"
      sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "PRAGMA table_info($T);" 2>/dev/null || true
      echo
    done

    echo "-- VIEWS --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='view' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no views)"
    echo

    echo "-- INDEXES --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='index' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no indexes)"
    echo

    echo "-- TRIGGERS --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='trigger' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no triggers)"
    echo
  } >> "$OUT"
done

# ---------- GIT PUSH ----------
cd "$ROOT"
git rev-parse --is-inside-work-tree >/dev/null 2>&1 || git init -q .
git config user.name "$GIT_USERNAME"
git config user.email "$GIT_EMAIL_USE"
git remote get-url origin >/dev/null 2>&1 || git remote add origin "$REMOTE_URL"

git add -f "$OUT"
git commit -m "dump ${TS}" || true
AUTH_URL="https://${GIT_USERNAME}:${GIT_TOKEN}@${REMOTE_URL#https://}"
git push -f "$AUTH_URL" HEAD:"$GIT_BRANCH"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/agg_3m_from_1m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

# Sécurité: vérifier que la base n'est pas verrouillée
if lsof "$DB" | grep -q ob.db; then
  echo "❌ ob.db en cours d'utilisation. Ferme les processus avant d'agréger."
  lsof "$DB"
  exit 1
fi

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;

-- (Optionnel mais recommandé si non créés) Index pour accélérer l'agrégation
-- CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ohlcv_1m_inst_ts ON ohlcv_1m(instId, ts);

-- Nettoyage 3m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;

-- Agrégation 1m -> 3m sans fonctions analytiques (compat SQLite 3.37)
WITH g AS (
  SELECT
    instId,
    (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts3,
    MIN(ts) AS ts_min,
    MAX(ts) AS ts_max,
    MAX(h) AS h,
    MIN(l) AS l,
    SUM(v) AS v
  FROM ohlcv_1m
  GROUP BY instId, ts3
)
INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m(instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
SELECT
  g.instId,
  g.ts3 AS ts,
  (SELECT o FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE instId=g.instId AND ts=g.ts_min) AS o,
  g.h,
  g.l,
  (SELECT c FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE instId=g.instId AND ts=g.ts_max) AS c,
  g.v
FROM g;

-- Vérification
SELECT '3m' AS tf, COUNT(*) AS rows, datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts
FROM ohlcv_3m;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_opener_health.sh -----
#!/bin/bash

DBG="/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db"
DBO="/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"

echo "=== OPENER HEALTH ==="

sqlite3 "$DBG" "
ATTACH '$DBO' AS op;

SELECT op.uid, g.status AS gest_status
FROM op.trades_open op
JOIN trades g ON g.uid = op.uid
WHERE g.status='opened';
"

echo
echo "-- Orphans (in opener but not in v_for_opener) --"
sqlite3 "$DBG" "
ATTACH '$DBO' AS op;
SELECT op.uid
FROM op.trades_open op
LEFT JOIN v_for_opener v ON v.uid = op.uid
WHERE v.uid IS NULL;
"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/cleanup_scalp_services.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "===== CLEANUP SCALP SERVICES ====="

SYSTEMD_DIR="/etc/systemd/system"

# Services SCALP valides qui NE DOIVENT PAS ÊTRE TOUCHÉS
KEEP=(
  scalp-ticks.service
  scalp-ob.service
  scalp-signal.service
  scalp-b-signals.service
  scalp-b-triggers.service
  scalp-opener.service
  scalp-follower.service
  scalp-closer.service
  scalp-recorder.service
  scalp-universe.service
  scalp-gest.service
  scalp-budget.service
)

KEEP_TIMERS=(
  scalp-ticks.timer
  scalp-ob.timer
  scalp-signal.timer
  scalp-b-feat.timer
  scalp-universe.timer
  scalp-maint-ohlcv.timer
  scalp-clean-signals.timer
  scalp-clean-tdb.timer
)

is_kept() {
  local item="$1"
  for k in "${KEEP[@]}" "${KEEP_TIMERS[@]}"; do
    if [[ "$k" == "$item" ]]; then
      return 0
    fi
  done
  return 1
}

# Trouver tous les services scalp*
echo
echo "--- SCALP SERVICES FOUND ---"
ALL=$(systemctl list-unit-files | grep -i scalp | awk '{print $1}')
echo "$ALL"

echo
echo "--- CLEANING UNUSED / FAILED ---"

for svc in $ALL; do
  if is_kept "$svc"; then
    echo "KEEP   $svc"
    continue
  fi

  # Vérifier s’il existe réellement sur disque
  if [[ ! -f "$SYSTEMD_DIR/$svc" ]]; then
    echo "REMOVE (phantom) $svc"
    systemctl disable "$svc" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    continue
  fi

  echo "DISABLE + DELETE $svc"
  systemctl stop "$svc" 2>/dev/null || true
  systemctl disable "$svc" 2>/dev/null || true
  rm -f "$SYSTEMD_DIR/$svc"
done

echo
echo "--- RELOADING SYSTEMD ---"
systemctl daemon-reload

echo "===== CLEANUP COMPLETE ====="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/clear_logs.sh -----
#!/bin/bash
LOGDIR="/opt/scalp/project/logs"

echo "=== CLEARING ALL SCALP LOGS IN ${LOGDIR} ==="

for f in ${LOGDIR}/*.log; do
    > "${f}"
    echo "Cleared: ${f}"
done

echo "=== DONE ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/closer_clean.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
sqlite3 "$DB" "DELETE FROM trades_close WHERE ts_close < (strftime('%s','now')-7200)*1000;"
sqlite3 "$DB" "VACUUM;"
echo "[CLEANER] closer.db compacted"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/dash.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/dash.log"
now_s=$(date +%s)
ts_now="$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
printf "\n===== SCALP PIPE HEALTH %s =====\n" "$(date '+%H:%M:%S')" | tee -a "$LOG"

check_db() {
    local name="$1" file="$2" table="$3" ts_col="$4"
    if [[ ! -f "$file" ]]; then
        printf "%-10s ❌ no DB found\n" "$name" | tee -a "$LOG"
        return
    fi
    local count ts_last age_s h m s age_hms status
    count=$(sqlite3 "$file" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;")
    ts_last=$(sqlite3 "$file" "SELECT MAX($ts_col)/1000 FROM $table;")
    [[ -z "$ts_last" || "$ts_last" == "0" ]] && ts_last=$now_s
    age_s=$(( now_s - ${ts_last%.*:-0} ))
    h=$((age_s/3600)); m=$(( (age_s%3600)/60 )); s=$((age_s%60))
    age_hms=$(printf "%02dh%02dm%02ds" "$h" "$m" "$s")

    if (( age_s < 10 )); then status="✅"
    elif (( age_s < 60 )); then status="⚠️"
    else status="❌"
    fi

    printf "%-10s %s  %4s recs | last=%s | age=%s\n" \
        "$name" "$status" "$count" "$(date '+%H:%M:%S' -d @$ts_last 2>/dev/null || date -r "$ts_last" '+%H:%M:%S')" "$age_hms" \
        | tee -a "$LOG"
}

check_db "opener"   "$DATA/opener.db"   "trades_open_init" "ts_create"
check_db "follower" "$DATA/follower.db" "trades_follow"    "ts_update"
check_db "closer"   "$DATA/closer.db"   "trades_close"     "ts_close"
check_db "recorder" "$DATA/recorder.db" "trades_record"    "ts_record"

printf "==============================================\n" | tee -a "$LOG"
echo "" >> "$LOG"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/dash_ob_feat.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

age() {
  ts_ms="$1"
  now_ms=$(($(date +%s) * 1000))
  echo $(( (now_ms - ts_ms) / 1000 ))
}

print_block() {
  local label="$1"
  echo "---- [$label] ----"
}

print_row() {
  local tf="$1"
  local rows="$2"
  local last_ts="$3"
  if [[ -z "$last_ts" || "$last_ts" == "0" ]]; then
      age_s="n/a"
  else
      age_s=$(age "$last_ts")
  fi
  printf "%-3s | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$tf" "$rows" "$age_s"
}

echo "==========================================="
echo "      MINI DASH — OB + FEAT (1m/3m/5m)"
echo "==========================================="

### OB ###
print_block "OB OHLCV"

for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    table="ohlcv_${tf}"
    rows=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;")
    last_ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM $table;")
    print_row "$tf" "$rows" "$last_ts"
done

### FEAT ###
print_block "FEAT"

for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    table="feat_${tf}"
    rows=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;")
    last_ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM $table;")
    print_row "$tf" "$rows" "$last_ts"
done

### STATUS ###
echo "---- [STATUS] ----"

ok=true
msg=""

# seuils
S1=120
S3=180
S5=300

check_tf() {
  local tf="$1"
  local ob_age="$2"
  local ft_age="$3"
  local max="$4"

  if (( ob_age > max )); then ok=false; msg="$msg ⚠️ OB ${tf} lag (${ob_age} s)\n"; fi
  if (( ft_age > max )); then ok=false; msg="$msg ⚠️ FEAT ${tf} lag (${ft_age} s)\n"; fi
}

ob1=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_1m;")")
ft1=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM feat_1m;")")

ob3=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_3m;")")
ft3=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM feat_3m;")")

ob5=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_5m;")")
ft5=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM feat_5m;")")

check_tf 1m "$ob1" "$ft1" "$S1"
check_tf 3m "$ob3" "$ft3" "$S3"
check_tf 5m "$ob5" "$ft5" "$S5"

if $ok; then
    echo "🟢 OK"
else
    echo -e "$msg"
fi

echo "==========================================="
echo "             FIN MINI DASH"
echo "==========================================="

.headers on
.mode column
SELECT ts,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS local,
       o,h,l,c,v
FROM ohlcv_${TF}
WHERE instId='${COIN}'
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

    echo
    echo "-------------------- FEAT $TF ------------------------"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT ts,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS local,
       c,
       ema12, ema26,
       macd, macdsignal, macdhist,
       rsi14_1m AS rsi,
       atr14  AS atr,
       bb_mid, bb_up, bb_low, bb_width,
       mom, roc, slope_ema12_1m AS slope,
       ctx
FROM feat_${TF}
WHERE instId='${COIN}'
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

done

echo "====================================================="
echo "                       END"
echo "====================================================="

#!/usr/bin/env bash

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] START maintenance" >>"$LOG"

DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_1m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 450
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_3m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_5m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
);
VACUUM;
SQL

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] CLEAN OK" >>"$LOG"

# --- Ré-agrégation 3m ---
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/agg_3m_from_1m.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || echo "agg_3m fail" >>"$LOG"

# --- Vérification fraîcheur ---

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] DONE maintenance" >>"$LOG"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_aggregate_3m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
LOCK="/var/lock/ob_agg3m.lock"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_agg3m.log"

exec /usr/bin/flock -n "$LOCK" bash -c "
  echo \"\$(date '+%F %T') [AGG3M] Start aggregation\" >> \$LOG
  sqlite3 \$DB '
    DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;
    INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m (instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
    SELECT instId,
           (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts_group,
           first_value(o) OVER w AS o,
           MAX(h) OVER w AS h,
           MIN(l) OVER w AS l,
           last_value(c) OVER w AS c,
           SUM(v) OVER w AS v
    FROM ohlcv_1m
    WINDOW w AS (PARTITION BY instId, (ts/180000) ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 2 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)
    GROUP BY instId, ts_group;
  '
  echo \"\$(date '+%F %T') [AGG3M] Done\" >> \$LOG
"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_freshness.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

# TF -> (table:limit_age)
declare -A TF_TABLES=(
    ["1m"]="ohlcv_1m:60"
    ["3m"]="ohlcv_3m:180"
    ["5m"]="ohlcv_5m:300"
)

now_ms=$(($(date +%s) * 1000))

echo "=== LAST OB CANDLES USED ==="
printf "%-3s %-19s %-7s %s\n" "tf" "last_ts" "age_s" "status"
echo "--  -------------------  -------  -------"

for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    entry="${TF_TABLES[$tf]}"
    table="${entry%%:*}"
    limit="${entry##*:}"

    last_ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM $table;")

    if [[ -z "$last_ts" || "$last_ts" == "NULL" ]]; then
        printf "%-3s %-19s %-7s %s\n" "$tf" "---" "---" "❌"
        continue
    fi

    age=$(( (now_ms - last_ts) / 1000 ))
    last_human=$(date -d "@$((last_ts / 1000))" +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

    status="⚠️"
    if (( age < limit )); then
        status="✅"
    fi

    printf "%-3s %-19s %-7d %s\n" "$tf" "$last_human" "$age" "$status"
done

LIMIT 8;
"

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# LAST TRADES BY STAGE
# ---------------------------------------------------------

echo "NEW:"
sqlite3 "$DB_G" "
.headers off
.mode column
SELECT uid, instId,
       datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
FROM trades
WHERE status='new'
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC LIMIT 5;
"

echo ""
echo "OPENED:"
sqlite3 "$DB_G" "
SELECT uid, instId,
       entry, qty,
       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')

WHERE status='opened'
ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 5;
"

SELECT uid, instId,
       sl_be, sl_trail, tp_dyn,

ORDER BY ts_follow DESC LIMIT 5;
"

SELECT uid, instId,
       price_to_close, reason_close,

FROM trades

"

ORDER BY ts_sync_close DESC LIMIT 5;
"
echo "$divider"

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# COHERENCE CHECK (TIMELINES)
# ---------------------------------------------------------
echo "[8] Timeline coherence check (ts_signal < ts_open < ts_follow < ts_close < ts_sync_close):"
sqlite3 "$DB_G" "
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT uid, instId,
       (ts_open     > ts_signal)     AS ok_open,
       (ts_follow   > ts_open)       AS ok_follow,
       (ts_close    > ts_follow)     AS ok_close,
       (ts_sync_close > ts_close)    AS ok_sync

WHERE status IN ('opened','follow','to_close','closed','recorded')

LIMIT 20;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/pipeline_diagnostics.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_O="/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"
DB_F="/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_C="/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

sqlite3 "$DB_C" <<'SQL'
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_O"' AS O;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_F"' AS F;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_B"' AS B;
.headers on
.mode column

WITH sig AS (
  SELECT instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_signal_s
  FROM B.signals_B
  GROUP BY instId
),
open AS (
  SELECT instId, MAX(ts_open) AS ts_open
  FROM O.trades_open_init
  GROUP BY instId
),
closed AS (
  SELECT instId, side, entry, exit, pnl, reason_exit, atr, ts_open, ts_close
  FROM main.positions_closed
)
SELECT
  c.instId,
  c.side,
  c.reason_exit,
  printf('%.4f', c.pnl) AS pnl,
  (c.ts_close - c.ts_open) AS trade_ms,
  CASE WHEN s.ts_signal_s IS NULL THEN NULL
       ELSE (c.ts_open - s.ts_signal_s*1000)
  END AS open_latency_ms
FROM closed c
LEFT JOIN sig s   ON s.instId = c.instId
LEFT JOIN open o  ON o.instId = c.instId AND o.ts_open = c.ts_open
ORDER BY c.ts_close DESC
LIMIT 50;

DETACH DATABASE O;
DETACH DATABASE F;
DETACH DATABASE B;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/pnl_live.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, time, os

DB_G = "/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db"
DB_T = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
DB_F = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"

def conn(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=2, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=2000;")
    return c

# ---------------------------------------
# TICKS
# ---------------------------------------
def get_ticks():
    con = conn(DB_T)
    rows = con.execute("SELECT instId, lastPr FROM v_ticks_latest;").fetchall()
    con.close()
    return {inst: price for inst, price in rows}

# ---------------------------------------
# TRADES EN COURS (gest)
# ---------------------------------------
def get_trades():
    con = conn(DB_G)
    rows = con.execute("""
    SELECT uid, instId, side, entry, qty, lev, margin, ts_open, status
    FROM trades
    WHERE status='opened' OR status='follow';
    """).fetchall()
    con.close()
    return rows

# ---------------------------------------
# SL/TP dynamiques (follower)
# ---------------------------------------
def get_dyn(uid):
    con = conn(DB_F)
    row = con.execute("""
        SELECT sl_be, sl_trail, tp_dyn, price_to_close
        FROM trades_follow
        WHERE uid=? AND status='follow'
        LIMIT 1;
    """,(uid,)).fetchone()
    con.close()

    if row is None:
        return None, None, None, None
    return row

# ---------------------------------------
# PNL
# ---------------------------------------
def compute_pnl(side, entry, qty, last):
    if last is None:
        return 0.0, 0.0

    if side == "buy":
        pnl = (last - entry) * qty
    else:
        pnl = (entry - last) * qty

    pct = (pnl / (entry * qty) * 100) if entry > 0 else 0
    return pnl, pct


# ---------------------------------------
# MAIN LOOP — refresh 1s
# ---------------------------------------
def main():

    while True:
        os.system("clear")

        ticks = get_ticks()
        trades = get_trades()

        print("")
        print("==============================================")
        print("          TRADES EN COURS — PnL LIVE          ")
        print("==============================================\n")

        print("{:23} {:10} {:5} {:10} {:10} {:10} {:10} {:10}".format(
            "uid", "instId", "side", "last", "pnl_usdt",
            "pnl_pct", "sl_dyn", "tp_dyn"
        ))
        print("-"*95)

        for uid, instId, side, entry, qty, lev, margin, ts_open, status in trades:

            inst_plain = instId.replace("/", "")
            last = ticks.get(inst_plain)

            pnl_usdt, pnl_pct = compute_pnl(side, entry, qty, last)

            sl_be, sl_trail, tp_dyn, price_to_close = get_dyn(uid)

            # sl_dyn = sl_trail (s'il existe), sinon sl_be
            sl_dyn = sl_trail if sl_trail else sl_be

            print("{:23} {:10} {:5} {:10.4f} {:10.4f} {:10.2f} {:10} {:10}".format(
                uid,
                instId,
                side,
                last if last else 0,
                pnl_usdt,
                pnl_pct,
                f"{sl_dyn:.4f}" if sl_dyn else "-",
                f"{tp_dyn:.4f}" if tp_dyn else "-"
            ))

        print("\n(rafraîchissement : 1 seconde)")
        time.sleep(1)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/rebuild_tdb_views.sh -----
#!/bin/bash
set -e

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

echo "[1] Dropping old views…"
sqlite3 "$DB" <<SQL
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_ticks_latest;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_hist_ordered;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_momentum_1;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_momentum_acc;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_atr;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_tick_classifier;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_ticks_for_follower;
SQL

echo "[2] Rebuilding views…"

sqlite3 "$DB" << 'SQL'

-- ============================================================
-- v_ticks_latest (1 ligne par instrument)
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW v_ticks_latest AS
SELECT
    t.instId,
    t.lastPr,
    t.ts_ms
FROM ticks t;


-- ============================================================
-- v_hist_ordered (historique par instrument)
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW v_hist_ordered AS
SELECT
    h.instId,
    h.lastPr,
    h.ts_ms,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
        PARTITION BY h.instId
        ORDER BY h.ts_ms DESC
    ) AS rn
FROM ticks_hist h;


-- ============================================================
-- momentum_1 : Δprice
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW v_momentum_1 AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    (l.lastPr - h.lastPr) AS momentum_1,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_hist_ordered h
    ON h.instId = l.instId AND h.rn = 1;


-- ============================================================
-- momentum_acc : somme glissante 10 ticks
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW v_momentum_acc AS
SELECT
    m.instId,
    m.ts_ms,
    (
        SELECT SUM(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr)
        FROM v_hist_ordered h2
        JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
            ON h3.instId = h2.instId
           AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
        WHERE h2.instId = m.instId
        AND h2.rn <= 10
    ) AS momentum_acc
FROM v_momentum_1 m;


-- ============================================================
-- ATR fast / slow
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW v_atr AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    -- fast ATR (10)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 10) AS atr_fast,

    -- slow ATR (30)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 30) AS atr_slow
FROM v_ticks_latest l;


-- ============================================================
-- class_signal
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW v_tick_classifier AS
SELECT
    a.instId,
    CASE
        WHEN a.atr_fast IS NULL THEN 'NEUTRAL'
        WHEN a.atr_fast > a.atr_slow * 1.8 THEN 'BREAKOUT'
        WHEN a.atr_fast < a.atr_slow * 0.4 THEN 'SQUEEZE'
        ELSE 'CHOP'
    END AS class_signal
FROM v_atr a;


-- ============================================================
-- v_ticks_for_follower : vue finale
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW v_ticks_for_follower AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    m1.momentum_1,
    COALESCE(macc.momentum_acc, 0) AS momentum_acc,
    a.atr_fast,
    a.atr_slow,
    0 AS pos_in_range,           -- volontairement ignoré (non utilisé)
    c.class_signal,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_1 m1 ON m1.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_acc macc ON macc.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_atr a ON a.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_tick_classifier c ON c.instId = l.instId;

SQL

echo "[3] Views rebuilt OK."

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/relaunch_ohlcv_feat.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "===== RELANCE OHLCV + FEAT ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="

# --- stop services ---
echo "[1] Stop services"
systemctl stop scalp-ob.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-oa.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-b-feat-builder.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-b-feat-builder.timer || true

# --- kill python leftover ---
echo "[2] Kill runaway processes"
pkill -f OB_collect.py || true
pkill -f OA_ohlcv_A.py || true
pkill -f B_feat_builder || true

# --- cleanup OHLCV if old ---
DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
echo "[3] Check OHLCV timestamps"

AGE1=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ohlcv_1m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)
AGE5=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ohlcv_5m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)

if (( AGE1 > 300 || AGE5 > 300 )); then
    echo "⚠️ OHLCV trop vieux → reset tables"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m;"
else
    echo "OK OHLCV pas trop vieux"
fi

# --- cleanup feat if old ---
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
echo "[4] Check FEAT timestamps"

F1=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM feat_1m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)

if (( F1 > 300 )); then
    echo "⚠️ Features trop vieux → reset feat tables"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_1m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_3m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_5m;"
fi

# --- restart pipeline ---
echo "[5] Restart OA"
systemctl start scalp-oa.service

echo "[6] Restart OB"
systemctl start scalp-ob.service

echo "[7] Restart feat builder (timer)"
systemctl start scalp-b-feat-builder.timer

echo "===== RELANCE OK ====="

echo "[8] Vérification dans 10 secondes…"
sleep 10

echo "--- OHLCV FRESHNESS ---"
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ohlcv_freshness.sh | sed 's/^/    /'

echo "--- FEAT FRESHNESS ---"
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_feat_freshness.sh | sed 's/^/    /'

#!/usr/bin/env bash

echo "=== RESTART A PIPELINE (OA → FEAT → CTX) ==="

SVC=(
  scalp-a-ctx.service
  scalp-a-feat.service
  scalp-oa.service
)

TMR=(
  scalp-a-ctx.timer
  scalp-a-feat.timer
  scalp-oa.timer
  scalp-a-pipeline.timer
)

echo "[1] Stop services..."
for s in "${SVC[@]}"; do
  systemctl stop "$s" 2>/dev/null || true
done

echo "[2] Stop timers..."
for t in "${TMR[@]}"; do
  systemctl stop "$t" 2>/dev/null || true
done

echo "[3] Reload systemd..."
systemctl daemon-reload

echo "[4] Start OA first..."
systemctl start scalp-oa.service

echo "[5] Start timers (pipeline)..."
systemctl start scalp-a-pipeline.timer

echo "=== DONE ==="
echo "Check: systemctl status scalp-a-pipeline.timer --no-pager"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/scalp_diag.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash

SERVICES=(
    scalp-u.service
    scalp-ticks.service
    scalp-ob.service
    scalp-oa.service
    scalp-a-ctx.service
    scalp-b-feat.service
    scalp-b-triggers.service
    scalp-signals.service
    scalp-opener.service
    scalp-follower.service
    scalp-closer.service
    scalp-recorder.service
    scalp-gest.service
)

echo "======================================================="
echo "           SCALP SYSTEMD HEALTH CHECK"
echo "======================================================="

for SVC in "${SERVICES[@]}"; do
    echo ""
    echo "-------------------------------------------------------"
    echo " Checking: $SVC"
    echo "-------------------------------------------------------"

    # Fichier unitaire présent ?
    if [ -f "/etc/systemd/system/$SVC" ] || [ -f "/lib/systemd/system/$SVC" ]; then
        echo "✓ Unit file present"
    else
        echo "✗ Unit file missing"
        continue
    fi

    # Masked ?
    MASKED=$(systemctl is-enabled "$SVC" 2>&1)
    if [[ "$MASKED" == "masked" ]]; then
        echo "✗ MASKED — must unmask: systemctl unmask $SVC"
        continue
    else
        echo "✓ Not masked"
    fi

    # Enabled ?
    ENABLED=$(systemctl is-enabled "$SVC" 2>/dev/null)
    if [[ "$ENABLED" == "enabled" ]]; then
        echo "✓ Enabled"
    else
        echo "✗ NOT enabled — run: systemctl enable $SVC"
    fi

    # Running / Active
    ACTIVE=$(systemctl is-active "$SVC" 2>/dev/null)
    if [[ "$ACTIVE" == "active" ]]; then
        echo "✓ Running"
    else
        echo "✗ NOT running — run: systemctl start $SVC"
    fi

    # Dernières erreurs
    echo ""
    echo "Last 3 log lines:"
    journalctl -u "$SVC" -n 3 --no-pager || echo "(no logs)"
done

echo ""
echo "======================================================="
echo "           END OF SCALP HEALTH CHECK"
echo "======================================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/sync_ctx_a_to_b.sql -----
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db' AS A;

-- Mise à jour de feat_1m.ctx avec le contexte réel de A
UPDATE feat_1m
SET ctx = (
    SELECT ctx_a.ctx
    FROM A.ctx_a_latest AS ctx_a
    WHERE REPLACE(ctx_a.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(feat_1m.instId,'/','')
)
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM A.ctx_a_latest AS ctx_a
    WHERE REPLACE(ctx_a.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(feat_1m.instId,'/','')
);

DETACH DATABASE A;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/t_db_clean.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

echo "===== CLEAN t.db WAL ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="

# Stop tick service
systemctl stop scalp-ticks.service 2>/dev/null || true
sleep 1

echo "[1] WAL FILES BEFORE"
ls -lh ${DB}*

echo "[2] CHECKPOINT WAL"
sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(FULL);"

echo "[3] Disable WAL"
sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA journal_mode=DELETE;"

echo "[4] VACUUM (compact file)"
sqlite3 "$DB" "VACUUM;"

echo "[5] Re-enable WAL"
sqlite3 "$DB" "PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;"

echo "[6] WAL FILES AFTER"
ls -lh ${DB}*

echo "===== CLEAN DONE ====="

systemctl start scalp-ticks.service 2>/dev/null || true

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ticks_loop.sh -----
#!/bin/bash

ROOT="/opt/scalp/project"
cd "$ROOT"

LOG="$ROOT/logs/ticks_loop.log"
PY="$ROOT/venv/bin/python3"
SCRIPT="$ROOT/scripts/ticks.py"

echo "[ticks-loop] Starting infinite supervisor..." >> "$LOG"

while true; do
    echo "[ticks-loop] Launching ticks.py at $(date)" >> "$LOG"
    nice -n 10 $PY $SCRIPT >> "$LOG" 2>&1
    EXITCODE=$?
    echo "[ticks-loop] ticks.py exited with code $EXITCODE at $(date)" >> "$LOG"
    sleep 1
done

    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
    open REAL,
    high REAL,
    low REAL,
    close REAL,
    volume REAL,
    PRIMARY KEY (instId, ts)
)
CREATE TABLE ohlcv_30m (
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
    open REAL,
    high REAL,
    low REAL,
    close REAL,
    volume REAL,
    PRIMARY KEY (instId, ts)
)
CREATE TABLE ohlcv_5m (
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
    open REAL,
    high REAL,
    low REAL,
    close REAL,
    volume REAL,
    PRIMARY KEY (instId, ts)
)
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq)
CREATE VIEW v_ohlcv_15m_latest AS
SELECT *
FROM ohlcv_15m
WHERE ts IN (
    SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_15m AS o2
    WHERE o2.instId = ohlcv_15m.instId
    ORDER BY ts DESC
    LIMIT 150
)
CREATE VIEW v_ohlcv_30m_latest AS
SELECT *
FROM ohlcv_30m
WHERE ts IN (
    SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_30m AS o2
    WHERE o2.instId = ohlcv_30m.instId
    ORDER BY ts DESC
    LIMIT 150
)
CREATE VIEW v_ohlcv_5m_latest AS
SELECT *
FROM ohlcv_5m
WHERE ts IN (
    SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_5m AS o2
    WHERE o2.instId = ohlcv_5m.instId
    ORDER BY ts DESC
    LIMIT 150
)

-- --- a.db ---
CREATE TABLE ctx_A (
    instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    ts_updated INTEGER,

    trend_5m   TEXT,
    trend_15m  TEXT,
    trend_30m  TEXT,

    score_5m   REAL,
    score_15m  REAL,
    score_30m  REAL,

    score_final REAL,

    p_buy  REAL,
    p_sell REAL,
    p_hold REAL,

    ctx TEXT
, score_A REAL DEFAULT 0.5)
CREATE TABLE feat_15m (

CREATE VIEW v_ctx_latest AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ctx,
    score_A AS score_C,
    ts_updated
FROM ctx_A
WHERE ts_updated = (
    SELECT MAX(ts_updated)
    FROM ctx_A c2
    WHERE c2.instId = ctx_A.instId
)
CREATE VIEW v_ctx_overview AS
SELECT
    instId,
    DATETIME(ts_updated/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts,
    score_5m,
    score_15m,
    score_30m,
    score_final,
    CASE
        WHEN score_final IS NOT NULL THEN
            ROUND( exp(score_final/0.35)
                / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35)), 6 )
    END AS p_buy,
    CASE
        WHEN score_final IS NOT NULL THEN
            ROUND( exp(-score_final/0.35)
                / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35)), 6 )
    END AS p_sell,
    CASE
        WHEN score_final IS NOT NULL THEN
            ROUND( 1
                - (exp(score_final/0.35)
                   / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35)))
                - (exp(-score_final/0.35)
                   / (exp(score_final/0.35) + 1 + exp(-score_final/0.35))), 6 )
    END AS p_hold,
    ctx
FROM ctx_A
ORDER BY instId
CREATE VIEW v_ohlcv_freshness AS
SELECT
    instId,
    MAX(ts) AS ts,
    (strftime('%s','now') * 1000 - MAX(ts)) AS age_ms
FROM ohlcv_5m
GROUP BY instId

-- --- budget.db ---
CREATE TABLE balance (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id = 1),
    balance_usdt REAL NOT NULL
)
CREATE TABLE budget_state(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id=1),
            balance REAL DEFAULT 1000.0,
            margin REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            pnl_real REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            ts_update INTEGER
        )
CREATE TABLE bus_out (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT,
    event TEXT,
    ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
    ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
, payload TEXT, src TEXT)
CREATE TABLE ledger (
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  src TEXT,
  instId TEXT,
  side TEXT,
  type TEXT,        -- margin / pnl_real / deposit / withdraw
  amount REAL,
  ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000)
)
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq)
CREATE VIEW v_balance AS
SELECT balance_usdt
FROM balance
WHERE id = 1
CREATE VIEW v_budget_overview AS
SELECT
  ROUND(balance,6) AS balance,
  ROUND(margin,6)  AS margin,
  ROUND(pnl_real,6) AS pnl_real,
  datetime(ts_update,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update
FROM budget_state
CREATE VIEW v_exposure AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='margin' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS margin,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='pnl_real' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS pnl_real
FROM ledger
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY ABS(margin) DESC

-- --- gest.db ---
CREATE TABLE gest (
    uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,

    instId TEXT NOT NULL,          -- Format: BTC/USDT
    side TEXT NOT NULL,            -- buy / sell

    ts_signal INTEGER NOT NULL,
    price_signal REAL DEFAULT 0,

    reason TEXT,                   -- Ex: TP_INIT, BREAKOUT
    entry_reason TEXT,             -- MOMENTUM / REVERSAL / …
    type_signal TEXT,              -- MOMENTUM / BREAKOUT / REVERSAL …

    score_C REAL,                  -- score contexte (Ctx)
    score_S REAL,                  -- score signal (Signal Strength)
    score_H REAL,                  -- score historique (Historical)

    entry REAL,
    qty REAL,
    lev REAL,
    margin REAL,

    ts_open INTEGER,
    sl_init REAL,
    tp_init REAL,

    ts_follow INTEGER,
    sl_be REAL,
    sl_trail REAL,
    tp_dyn REAL,

    price_to_close REAL,

    ts_close INTEGER,
    price_close REAL,
    reason_close TEXT,
    ctx_close TEXT,

    price_exec_close REAL,
    pnl REAL,
    pnl_pct REAL,
    fee_open REAL,
    fee_close REAL,
    fee_total REAL,
    pnl_net REAL,

    wt_delta_t_ms INTEGER,
    wt_delta_price_pct REAL,
    wt_peak_ts INTEGER,
    wt_peak_price REAL,

    status TEXT NOT NULL,          -- new / opened / follow / to_close / closed / recorded
    ts_status_update INTEGER
, atr_signal REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0)
CREATE TABLE trades (
    uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    side TEXT NOT NULL,

    ts_signal INTEGER NOT NULL,
    price_signal REAL NOT NULL,

    reason TEXT NOT NULL,
    entry_reason TEXT,
    type_signal TEXT,

    score_C REAL,
    score_S REAL,
    score_H REAL,

    entry REAL,
    qty REAL,
    lev REAL,
    margin REAL,

    ts_open INTEGER,
    sl_init REAL,
    tp_init REAL,

    ts_follow INTEGER,
    sl_be REAL,
    sl_trail REAL,
    tp_dyn REAL,

    price_to_close REAL,
    ts_close INTEGER,
    price_close REAL,
    reason_close TEXT,
    price_exec_close REAL,

    pnl REAL,
    pnl_pct REAL,
    fee_open REAL,
    fee_close REAL,
    fee_total REAL,
    pnl_net REAL,

    ctx_close TEXT,

    wt_delta_t_ms INTEGER,
    wt_delta_price_pct REAL,
    wt_peak_ts INTEGER,
    wt_peak_price REAL,

    status TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts_status_update INTEGER
)
CREATE VIEW v_gest AS
SELECT *
FROM gest
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
CREATE VIEW v_gest_status_count AS
SELECT status, COUNT(*) AS n
FROM gest
GROUP BY status
ORDER BY
    CASE status
        WHEN 'new'       THEN 1
        WHEN 'opened'    THEN 2
        WHEN 'follow'    THEN 3
        WHEN 'to_close'  THEN 4
        WHEN 'closed'    THEN 5
        WHEN 'recorded'  THEN 6
        ELSE 99
    END

        ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
      )

            instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            avg_pnl REAL,
            winrate REAL,
            trades INTEGER,
            last_update INTEGER
        )
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq)

-- --- t.db ---
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq)
CREATE TABLE ticks (
    instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    lastPr REAL NOT NULL,
    ts_ms INTEGER NOT NULL
)
CREATE TABLE ticks_hist (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    lastPr REAL NOT NULL,
    ts_ms INTEGER NOT NULL
)
CREATE VIEW v_atr AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    -- fast ATR (10)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 10) AS atr_fast,

    -- slow ATR (30)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 30) AS atr_slow
FROM v_ticks_latest l
CREATE VIEW v_hist_ordered AS
SELECT
    h.instId,
    h.lastPr,
    h.ts_ms,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
        PARTITION BY h.instId
        ORDER BY h.ts_ms DESC
    ) AS rn
FROM ticks_hist h
CREATE VIEW v_momentum_1 AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    (l.lastPr - h.lastPr) AS momentum_1,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_hist_ordered h
    ON h.instId = l.instId AND h.rn = 1
CREATE VIEW v_momentum_acc AS
SELECT
    m.instId,
    m.ts_ms,
    (
        SELECT SUM(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr)
        FROM v_hist_ordered h2
        JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
            ON h3.instId = h2.instId
           AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
        WHERE h2.instId = m.instId
        AND h2.rn <= 10
    ) AS momentum_acc
FROM v_momentum_1 m
CREATE VIEW v_tick_classifier AS
SELECT
    a.instId,
    CASE
        WHEN a.atr_fast IS NULL THEN 'NEUTRAL'
        WHEN a.atr_fast > a.atr_slow * 1.8 THEN 'BREAKOUT'
        WHEN a.atr_fast < a.atr_slow * 0.4 THEN 'SQUEEZE'
        ELSE 'CHOP'
    END AS class_signal
FROM v_atr a
CREATE VIEW v_tick_range AS
SELECT instId,
       ABS(lastPr - prevPr) AS tr,
       ts_ms
FROM v_hist_ordered
WHERE prevPr IS NOT NULL
CREATE VIEW v_tick_range_position AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT instId,lastPr,ts_ms,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms DESC) rn
    FROM ticks_hist
),
range_win AS (
    SELECT instId,lastPr FROM base WHERE rn <= 26
),
agg AS (
    SELECT instId, MIN(lastPr) AS minP, MAX(lastPr) AS maxP
    FROM range_win GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT
   t.instId,
   t.lastPr,
   t.ts_ms,
   CASE WHEN a.maxP = a.minP THEN 0.5
        ELSE (t.lastPr - a.minP)/(a.maxP - a.minP)
   END AS pos_in_range
FROM ticks t
JOIN agg a USING(instId)
CREATE VIEW v_tick_volatility AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        ts_ms,
        ABS(lastPr - LAG(lastPr) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms)) AS tr,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms DESC) AS rn
    FROM ticks_hist
)
SELECT
    instId,
    AVG(CASE WHEN rn <= 11 THEN tr END) AS atr_fast,
    AVG(CASE WHEN rn <= 26 THEN tr END) AS atr_slow
FROM base
GROUP BY instId
CREATE VIEW v_ticks_for_follower AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    m1.momentum_1,
    COALESCE(macc.momentum_acc, 0) AS momentum_acc,
    a.atr_fast,
    a.atr_slow,
    0 AS pos_in_range,           -- volontairement ignoré (non utilisé)
    c.class_signal,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_1 m1 ON m1.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_acc macc ON macc.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_atr a ON a.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_tick_classifier c ON c.instId = l.instId
CREATE VIEW v_ticks_latest AS
SELECT
    t.instId,
    t.lastPr,
    t.ts_ms
FROM ticks t

-- --- u.db ---
CREATE TABLE bus_out(
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        src TEXT,
        instId TEXT,
        event TEXT,
        payload TEXT DEFAULT '{}',
        ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
        ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
      )
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq)
CREATE TABLE universe(
  instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY
, score_U REAL DEFAULT 0, active INTEGER DEFAULT 1, enabled INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1)

-- --- triggers.db ---
CREATE TABLE sqlite_sequence(name,seq)
CREATE TABLE trig_state (
    instId     TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    reason     TEXT,
    side       TEXT,
    score      REAL,
    ts         INTEGER
)
CREATE TABLE triggers (
    id          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId      TEXT    NOT NULL,
    tf          TEXT    NOT NULL,           -- timeframe (ex: '1m')
    side        TEXT    NOT NULL,           -- 'buy' / 'sell'
    reason      TEXT    NOT NULL,           -- type de trigger
    score       REAL    NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, -- score brut du trigger
    ctx         TEXT,                       -- contexte (optionnel)
    confidence  REAL    NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, -- réserve si tu veux
    price       REAL,                       -- lastPr au moment du trigger
    atr         REAL,                       -- ATR utilisé (optionnel)
    ts          INTEGER NOT NULL,           -- timestamp ms
    consumed    INTEGER DEFAULT 0           -- 0 = non pris, 1 = consommé
)
CREATE VIEW v_triggers_latest AS
WITH last_ts AS (
    SELECT instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_last
    FROM triggers
    GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT
    t.instId,
    t.side,
    t.reason,
    t.score   AS score_B,
    t.ctx,
    t.price,
    t.atr,
    t.ts      AS ts_trigger
FROM triggers t
JOIN last_ts lt
  ON lt.instId = t.instId AND lt.ts_last = t.ts
ORDER BY t.ts DESC

-- --- signals.db ---
CREATE TABLE signals (
    trade_uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    instId    TEXT NOT NULL,
    side      TEXT NOT NULL,
    reason    TEXT NOT NULL,
    ctx       TEXT,
    score_A   REAL,
    score_B   REAL,
    price     REAL NOT NULL,
    atr       REAL,
    ts_signal INTEGER NOT NULL,
    ts_local  TEXT,
    hms       TEXT
)
CREATE VIEW v_for_gest AS
SELECT
    s.trade_uid AS uid,
    s.instId,
    s.side,
    s.reason,
    s.ctx,
    s.score_A,
    s.score_B,
    s.price AS price_signal,
    s.atr   AS atr_signal,
    s.ts_signal
FROM signals s
JOIN (
    SELECT instId, MAX(ts_signal) AS max_ts
    FROM signals
    GROUP BY instId
) x ON x.instId = s.instId
   AND x.max_ts = s.ts_signal
ORDER BY s.ts_signal DESC

-- --- opener.db ---
CREATE TABLE opener (
    uid     TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    ts_open INTEGER,
    entry   REAL,
    qty     REAL,
    lev     REAL,
    margin  REAL,
    status  TEXT
)
CREATE TABLE trades_open (
    uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,

    instId TEXT,
    side TEXT,

    entry REAL,
    qty REAL,
    lev REAL,
    margin REAL,

    sl_init REAL,
    tp_init REAL,

    ts_open INTEGER,
    status TEXT
)
CREATE VIEW v_opener AS
SELECT
    uid,
    ts_open,
    entry,
    qty,
    lev,
    margin,
    status
FROM opener
CREATE VIEW v_opener_for_gest AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    side,
    entry,
    qty,
    lev,
    margin,
    sl_init,
    tp_init,
    ts_open,
    status
FROM trades_open
WHERE status IN ('opened', 'skipped')
ORDER BY ts_open ASC

-- --- follower.db ---
CREATE TABLE follower(
    uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    ts_follow INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    sl_be REAL DEFAULT 0,
    sl_trail REAL DEFAULT 0,
    tp_dyn REAL DEFAULT 0,
    atr_signal REAL DEFAULT 0,
    status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'follow'
)
CREATE VIEW v_follower AS
SELECT
    uid,
    ts_follow,
    sl_be,
    sl_trail,
    tp_dyn,
    atr_signal,
    status
FROM follower
ORDER BY ts_follow DESC

-- --- closer.db ---
CREATE TABLE closer (
    uid              TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    ts_close         INTEGER,
    price_exec_close REAL,
    pnl              REAL,
    pnl_pct          REAL,
    fee              REAL,
    reason_close     TEXT,
    ctx_close        TEXT,
    status           TEXT
)
CREATE TABLE trades_close (
    uid       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    instId    TEXT NOT NULL,
    price_exec REAL NOT NULL,
    ts_exec    INTEGER NOT NULL
)
CREATE VIEW v_closer AS
SELECT
    uid,
    ts_close,
    price_exec_close,
    pnl,
    pnl_pct,
    fee,
    reason_close,
    ctx_close,
    status
FROM closer
CREATE VIEW v_closer_for_gest AS
SELECT
    uid,
    ts_exec      AS ts_close,
    price_exec   AS price_close,
    NULL         AS pnl_usdt,
    NULL         AS pnl_pct,
    'closed'     AS status,
    NULL         AS reason_close
FROM trades_close
ORDER BY ts_exec ASC

-- --- recorder.db ---
CREATE TABLE recorder (
    uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    side TEXT NOT NULL,

    ts_signal INTEGER NOT NULL,
    price_signal REAL NOT NULL,
    entry_reason TEXT,
    type_signal TEXT,
    score_C REAL,
    score_S REAL,

    ts_open INTEGER,
    entry REAL,
    qty REAL,
    lev REAL,
    margin REAL,

    ts_close INTEGER,
    price_close REAL,
    reason_close TEXT,

    pnl REAL,
    pnl_pct REAL,
    pnl_net REAL,
    fee REAL,

    ctx_close TEXT,

    -- wticks analytics
    wt_delta_t_ms INTEGER,
    wt_delta_price_pct REAL,
    wt_peak_ts INTEGER,
    wt_peak_price REAL,

    ts_recorded INTEGER NOT NULL
, fee_total REAL DEFAULT 0)
CREATE TABLE records (
    uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    instId TEXT,
    side TEXT,
    entry REAL,
    qty REAL,
    lev REAL,
    margin REAL,
    sl REAL,
    tp REAL,
    ts_open INTEGER,
    ts_follow INTEGER,
    sl_be REAL,
    sl_trail REAL,
    tp_dyn REAL,
    price_to_close REAL,
    ts_close INTEGER,
    price_close REAL,
    status TEXT,
    reason TEXT,
    ctx TEXT,
    score_A REAL,
    score_B REAL,
    ts_signal INTEGER,
    atr_signal REAL,
    price_signal REAL,
    ts_status_update INTEGER,
    reason_close TEXT,
    price_exec_close REAL,
    pnl REAL,

)

, tp_dyn REAL, price_to_close REAL, pnl REAL, ts_sync_close INTEGER)

, ts_peak INTEGER, price_peak REAL, delta_t_ms INTEGER, delta_price REAL, delta_price_pct REAL, score_T REAL)

    uid,

FROM recorder

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_analyse.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, math, time

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_U = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
TF = "5m"

def softmax(x):
    e = [math.exp(i) for i in x]
    s = sum(e)
    return [v/s for v in e]

def get_universe():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_U)
    rows = con.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe ORDER BY instId").fetchall()
    con.close()
    return [r[0] for r in rows]

def load_ob(inst):
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_OB)
    row = con.execute(f"SELECT rsi FROM ob_{TF} WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1", (inst,)).fetchone()
    con.close()
    return row[0] if row else None

def compute_ctx(rsi):
    if rsi < 30: return "bullish"
    if rsi > 70: return "bearish"
    if 45 <= rsi <= 55: return "range"
    return "none"

def compute_score_A(ctx):
    if ctx == "bullish": return 0.8
    if ctx == "bearish": return -0.8
    if ctx == "range": return 0.0
    return 0.0

def run():
    insts = get_universe()
    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    out = []

    for inst in insts:
        rsi = load_ob(inst)
        if rsi is None:
            continue
        ctx = compute_ctx(rsi)
        score_A = compute_score_A(ctx)
        p_buy, p_sell = softmax([score_A, -score_A])
        out.append((inst, now, 0.0, score_A, p_buy, p_sell, ctx))

    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    con.execute("DELETE FROM ctx_a_latest")
    con.executemany("INSERT INTO ctx_a_latest(instId,ts,score_U,score_A,p_buy,p_sell,ctx) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)", out)
    con.commit()
    con.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run()

W_SHORT = 0.50
