#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio, json, time, websockets

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
INSTRUMENTS = ["BTCUSDT", "ETHUSDT", "BNBUSDT"]

async def test():
    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=None) as ws:
        subs = [{"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "ticker", "instId": i} for i in INSTRUMENTS]
        msg = {"op": "subscribe", "args": subs}
        await ws.send(json.dumps(msg))
        print("✅ Sent:", msg)

        async def pinger():
            while True:
                await asyncio.sleep(10)
                await ws.send('{"op":"ping"}')
        asyncio.create_task(pinger())

        while True:
            raw = await ws.recv()
            ts = time.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            print(f"\n[{ts}] RAW →", raw[:250])

            try:
                data = json.loads(raw)
                if "data" in data:
                    for d in data["data"]:
                        inst = d.get("instId")
                        pr   = d.get("lastPr")
                        if inst and pr:
                            print(f"→ Parsed {inst} = {pr}")
            except Exception as e:
                print("⚠️ Parse error:", e)

asyncio.run(test())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/U_universe.py -----
import ccxt, sqlite3

DBU = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
TOP = 20

exchange = ccxt.bitget()
markets = exchange.load_markets()

perps = []
for s,info in markets.items():
    if info.get('swap',False) and info['quote'] == 'USDT':
        inst = s.replace(":USDT","")  # -> BTC/USDT:USDT → BTC/USDT
        perps.append(inst)

perps = perps[:TOP]

con = sqlite3.connect(DBU, timeout=5)
con.execute("DELETE FROM universe;")
for inst in perps:
    con.execute("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO universe(instId) VALUES (?)", (inst,))
con.commit()
con.close()

print("[U] OK :", perps)

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/WS_candles_to_wsdb.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio
import json
import sqlite3
import websockets
import time
from datetime import datetime

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

DB_WS = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ws.db"
DB_U  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

TF = {
    "candle5m":  5  * 60 * 1000,
    "candle15m": 15 * 60 * 1000,
    "candle30m": 30 * 60 * 1000
}

###############################################################################
# DB Helpers
###############################################################################
def load_universe():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_U)
    rows = conn.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe ORDER BY instId;").fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return [r[0] for r in rows]

def wsdb_conn():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_WS, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return conn

###############################################################################
# WS Subscription builder
###############################################################################
def build_sub(universe):
    args = []
    for instId in universe:
        args.append({"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle5m","instId":instId})
        args.append({"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle15m","instId":instId})
        args.append({"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle30m","instId":instId})
    return {"op":"subscribe", "args":args}

###############################################################################
# Insert into WS DB (closed candles only)
###############################################################################
def insert_ws_candle(conn, table, instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v):
    conn.execute(
        f"""
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table}(instId, ts, open, high, low, close, volume)
        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """,
        (instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
    )

###############################################################################
# Main WebSocket loop
###############################################################################
async def run_ws():
    universe = load_universe()
    sub = build_sub(universe)

    ws_conn = wsdb_conn()

    while True:
        try:
            print("[WS] Connecting...")
            async with websockets.connect(
                WS_URL,
                ping_interval=None,
                ping_timeout=None,
                close_timeout=1
            ) as ws:

                print("[WS] Connected, subscribing…")
                await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))

                async def keep_alive():
                    while True:
                        await asyncio.sleep(15)
                        try:
                            await ws.send(json.dumps({"event":"ping"}))
                        except:
                            break

                asyncio.create_task(keep_alive())

                while True:
                    raw = await ws.recv()
                    data = json.loads(raw)

                    # Skip ping/pong
                    if isinstance(data, dict) and data.get("event") in ("ping","pong"):
                        continue

                    if "arg" not in data or "data" not in data:
                        continue

                    channel = data["arg"]["channel"]
                    instId  = data["arg"]["instId"]
                    rows    = data["data"]

                    if channel not in TF:
                        continue

                    tf_ms = TF[channel]
                    table = f"ws_ohlcv_{channel.replace('candle','')}"  # candle5m -> ws_ohlcv_5m

                    for k in rows:
                        ts = int(k[0])

                        # Only take closed candles
                        if ts % tf_ms != 0:
                            continue

                        o = float(k[1])
                        h = float(k[2])
                        l = float(k[3])
                        c = float(k[4])
                        v = float(k[5])

                        insert_ws_candle(ws_conn, table, instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)

                        print(
                            f"[WS] CLOSED {channel} {instId} "
                            f"ts={ts} o={o} h={h} l={l} c={c} v={v}"
                        )

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[WS] Error: {e}, retry in 5s…")
            await asyncio.sleep(5)

###############################################################################
# Entrypoint
###############################################################################
if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(run_ws())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/WS_multi_candles.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio
import json
import websockets
import sqlite3
import time

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
DB_U = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

# Timeframes in ms for identifying CLOSED candles
TF = {
    "candle5m":  5 * 60 * 1000,
    "candle15m": 15 * 60 * 1000,
    "candle30m": 30 * 60 * 1000
}

################################################################
# Load universe from u.db
################################################################
def load_universe():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_U)
    rows = conn.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe ORDER BY instId;").fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return [r[0] for r in rows]


################################################################
# Build subscription message
################################################################
def build_sub(universe):
    args = []
    for inst in universe:
        args.append({"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle5m","instId":inst})
        args.append({"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle15m","instId":inst})
        args.append({"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle30m","instId":inst})
    return {"op":"subscribe","args":args}


################################################################
# Core WS loop
################################################################
async def ws_loop():
    universe = load_universe()
    sub = build_sub(universe)

    while True:
        try:
            print("[WS] Connecting...")
            async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=20) as ws:
                print("[WS] Connected, subscribing…")
                await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))

                while True:
                    raw = await ws.recv()
                    data = json.loads(raw)

                    # Ignore heartbeats
                    if isinstance(data, dict) and data.get("event") in ("ping","pong"):
                        continue

                    # Only candle messages
                    if "arg" not in data or "data" not in data:
                        continue

                    channel = data["arg"].get("channel")
                    inst    = data["arg"].get("instId")
                    rows    = data["data"]

                    if channel not in TF:
                        continue

                    tf_ms = TF[channel]

                    # Process each kline
                    for k in rows:
                        ts     = int(k[0])
                        open_  = float(k[1])
                        high   = float(k[2])
                        low    = float(k[3])
                        close  = float(k[4])
                        volume = float(k[5])

                        # === FILTER: closed candles only ===
                        if ts % tf_ms != 0:
                            continue

                        print(f"[{channel}] CLOSED {inst}  ts={ts}  "
                              f"open={open_} high={high} low={low} "
                              f"close={close} vol={volume}")

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[WS] Error: {e}, retry in 5s…")
            await asyncio.sleep(5)


################################################################
# Entry point
################################################################
if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(ws_loop())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/analyse_recorded.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3
import argparse
import statistics
from datetime import datetime

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project"
DB_R = f"{ROOT}/data/recorder.db"

# ============================================================
# UTIL
# ============================================================

def conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_R, timeout=4, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=3000;")
    return c

def ms_to_dt(ms):
    try:
        return datetime.fromtimestamp(ms/1000).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    except:
        return "-"

def duration_s(ts_open, ts_close):
    if ts_open is None or ts_close is None:
        return None
    try:
        return round((ts_close - ts_open) / 1000, 3)
    except:
        return None

def hour_of(ms):
    try:
        return int(datetime.fromtimestamp(ms/1000).strftime("%H"))
    except:
        return None

# ============================================================
# FORMATTERS ROBUSTES
# ============================================================

def fmt(x, n=4):
    """Format numérique sûr : renvoie '-' si None."""
    if x is None:
        return "-"
    try:
        return f"{x:.{n}f}"
    except:
        return "-"

def fmt_dur(d):
    if d is None:
        return "-"
    try:
        return f"{d:.2f}"
    except:
        return "-"

# ============================================================
# FETCH FROM RECORDER (36 colonnes)
# ============================================================

def load_records(inst=None):
    c = conn()

    q = """
        SELECT
            uid,             -- 0
            instId,          -- 1
            side,            -- 2
            entry,           -- 3
            qty,             -- 4
            lev,             -- 5
            margin,          -- 6
            sl_init,         -- 7
            tp_init,         -- 8
            ts_open,         -- 9
            ts_follow,       -- 10
            sl_be,           -- 11
            sl_trail,        -- 12
            tp_dyn,          -- 13
            price_to_close,  -- 14
            ts_close,        -- 15
            price_close,     -- 16
            status,          -- 17
            reason,          -- 18
            ctx,             -- 19
            score_A,         -- 20
            score_B,         -- 21
            ts_signal,       -- 22
            atr_signal,      -- 23
            price_signal,    -- 24
            ts_status_update,-- 25
            reason_close,    -- 26
            price_exec_close,-- 27
            pnl,             -- 28
            ctx_close,       -- 29
            ts_sync_close,   -- 30
            pnl_pct,         -- 31
            fee_open,        -- 32
            fee_close,       -- 33
            fee_total,       -- 34
            pnl_net          -- 35
        FROM trades_recorded
    """

    params = []
    if inst:
        q += " WHERE instId=?"
        params.append(inst)

    q += " ORDER BY ts_close ASC;"

    rows = c.execute(q, params).fetchall()
    c.close()
    return rows

# ============================================================
# ANALYSE STATISTIQUE
# ============================================================

def compute_stats(rows):
    if not rows:
        return {}

    pnl = [r[28] for r in rows if r[28] is not None]
    pnl_net = [r[35] for r in rows if r[35] is not None]
    pct = [r[31] for r in rows if r[31] is not None]

    durations = [duration_s(r[9], r[15]) for r in rows if duration_s(r[9], r[15]) is not None]

    stats = {
        "count": len(rows),
        "pnl_total": sum(pnl) if pnl else 0,
        "pnl_net_total": sum(pnl_net) if pnl_net else 0,
        "pnl_avg": statistics.mean(pnl) if pnl else 0,
        "pnl_net_avg": statistics.mean(pnl_net) if pnl_net else 0,
        "pct_avg": statistics.mean(pct) if pct else 0,
        "wins": len([x for x in pnl_net if x > 0]),
        "losses": len([x for x in pnl_net if x <= 0]),
        "winrate": (len([x for x in pnl_net if x > 0]) / len(pnl_net) * 100) if pnl_net else 0,

        # Durées
        "dur_avg": statistics.mean(durations) if durations else 0.0,
        "dur_med": statistics.median(durations) if durations else 0.0,
        "dur_min": min(durations) if durations else 0.0,
        "dur_max": max(durations) if durations else 0.0,
    }

    # max drawdown
    cum = 0
    peak = 0
    dd = 0
    for p in pnl_net:
        cum += p
        peak = max(peak, cum)
        dd = min(dd, cum - peak)

    stats["max_drawdown"] = dd
    return stats

# ============================================================
# ANALYSE DURÉES PAR INTERVALLE
# ============================================================

def analyse_durations(rows):
    durations = [duration_s(r[9], r[15]) for r in rows if duration_s(r[9], r[15]) is not None]

    buckets = {
        "0–5s": 0,
        "5–15s": 0,
        "15–30s": 0,
        "30–60s": 0,
        "1–5min": 0,
        ">5min": 0,
    }

    for d in durations:
        if d <= 5: buckets["0–5s"] += 1
        elif d <= 15: buckets["5–15s"] += 1
        elif d <= 30: buckets["15–30s"] += 1
        elif d <= 60: buckets["30–60s"] += 1
        elif d <= 300: buckets["1–5min"] += 1
        else: buckets[">5min"] += 1

    print("=== DISTRIBUTION DES DURÉES ===")
    for k, v in buckets.items():
        print(f"{k:<10} : {v} trades")
    print("")

# ============================================================
# ANALYSE DURÉE PAR RAISON
# ============================================================

def analyse_duration_by_reason(rows):
    d = {}
    for r in rows:
        reason = r[26] or r[18] or "UNKNOWN"
        dur = duration_s(r[9], r[15])
        if dur is None:
            continue

        if reason not in d:
            d[reason] = []
        d[reason].append(dur)

    print("=== DURÉE MOYENNE PAR RAISON ===")
    for reason, ds in sorted(d.items(), key=lambda x: statistics.mean(x[1])):
        print(f"{reason:<25} Durée moy: {statistics.mean(ds):.2f}s  (n={len(ds)})")
    print("")

# ============================================================
# ANALYSE PAR RAISON DE SORTIE
# ============================================================

def analyse_reason(rows):
    d = {}
    for r in rows:
        reason = r[26] or r[18] or "UNKNOWN"
        pnl = r[35] if r[35] is not None else 0
        win = 1 if pnl > 0 else 0

        if reason not in d:
            d[reason] = {"count": 0, "wins": 0, "pnl": 0.0}

        d[reason]["count"] += 1
        d[reason]["wins"] += win
        d[reason]["pnl"] += pnl

    print("=== PERFORMANCE PAR RAISON DE SORTIE ===")
    for k, v in sorted(d.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1]["pnl"]):
        wr = (v["wins"] / v["count"] * 100) if v["count"] else 0
        print(f"{k:<25} Trades={v['count']:<4}  WinRate={wr:>5.1f}%   PNL Net={v['pnl']:+.4f}")
    print("")

# ============================================================
# BUY VS SELL
# ============================================================

def analyse_side(rows):
    d = {"buy": {"count": 0, "wins": 0, "pnl": 0.0},
         "sell": {"count": 0, "wins": 0, "pnl": 0.0}}

    for r in rows:
        side = r[2]
        pnl = r[35] if r[35] is not None else 0
        win = 1 if pnl > 0 else 0

        if side not in d:
            continue

        d[side]["count"] += 1
        d[side]["wins"] += win
        d[side]["pnl"] += pnl

    print("=== PERFORMANCE BUY VS SELL ===")
    for side in ["buy", "sell"]:
        c = d[side]["count"]
        wr = (d[side]["wins"] / c * 100) if c else 0
        print(f"{side.upper():<5} Trades={c:<4} WinRate={wr:>5.1f}%  PNL Net={d[side]['pnl']:+.4f}")
    print("")

# ============================================================
# PAR INSTRUMENT
# ============================================================

def analyse_inst(rows):
    d = {}
    for r in rows:
        inst = r[1]
        pnl = r[35] if r[35] is not None else 0
        win = 1 if pnl > 0 else 0

        if inst not in d:
            d[inst] = {"count": 0, "wins": 0, "pnl": 0.0}

        d[inst]["count"] += 1
        d[inst]["wins"] += win
        d[inst]["pnl"] += pnl

    print("=== PERFORMANCE PAR INSTRUMENT ===")
    for inst, v in sorted(d.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1]["pnl"]):
        wr = v["wins"] / v["count"] * 100 if v["count"] else 0
        print(f"{inst:<10} Trades={v['count']:<4} WinRate={wr:>5.1f}%  PNL Net={v['pnl']:+.4f}")
    print("")

# ============================================================
# PAR HEURE
# ============================================================

def analyse_hours(rows):
    d = {}
    for r in rows:
        hour = hour_of(r[9])
        pnl = r[35] if r[35] is not None else 0
        if hour not in d:
            d[hour] = {"count": 0, "pnl": 0.0}
        d[hour]["count"] += 1
        d[hour]["pnl"] += pnl

    print("=== PERFORMANCE PAR HEURE ===")
    for h, v in sorted(d.items()):
        print(f"Heure {h:02d} : Trades={v['count']:<4}  PNL Net={v['pnl']:+.4f}")
    print("")

# ============================================================
# TABLE DISPLAY
# ============================================================

def display_table(rows):
    print("================================================================================================")
    print("                               ANALYSE DES TRADES ENREGISTRES (LEDGER)                           ")
    print("================================================================================================")
    print("")
    print(f"{'uid':<22} {'inst':<10} {'side':<5} {'entry':>8} {'exit':>8} {'pnl_net':>10} {'pct':>7} {'dur(s)':>7} {'reason':<18} {'open':<19} {'close':<19}")
    print("-" * 150)

    for r in rows:
        uid         = r[0]
        inst        = r[1]
        side        = r[2]
        entry       = r[3]
        price_close = r[16]
        pnl_net     = r[35]
        pnl_pct     = r[31]
        reason      = r[26] or r[18] or "UNKNOWN"
        ts_open     = r[9]
        ts_close    = r[15]
        dur         = duration_s(ts_open, ts_close)

        print(
            f"{uid:<22} "
            f"{inst:<10} "
            f"{side:<5} "
            f"{fmt(entry):>8} "
            f"{fmt(price_close):>8} "
            f"{fmt(pnl_net):>10} "
            f"{fmt(pnl_pct,3):>7} "
            f"{fmt_dur(dur):>7} "
            f"{reason:<18} "
            f"{ms_to_dt(ts_open):<19} "
            f"{ms_to_dt(ts_close):<19}"
        )

    print("")

# ============================================================
# GLOBAL STATS DISPLAY
# ============================================================

def display_stats(stats):
    print("================================ STATISTIQUES =================================")
    print(f"Total trades       : {stats['count']}")
    print(f"Win rate           : {stats['winrate']:.2f} %")
    print(f"PNL total          : {stats['pnl_total']:.4f}")
    print(f"PNL NET total      : {stats['pnl_net_total']:.4f}")
    print(f"PNL net moyen      : {stats['pnl_net_avg']:.4f}")
    print(f"PNL % moyen        : {stats['pct_avg']:.4f}")
    print(f"Max drawdown       : {stats['max_drawdown']:.4f}")
    print("")
    print(f"Durée moyenne      : {stats['dur_avg']:.2f} s")
    print(f"Durée médiane      : {stats['dur_med']:.2f} s")
    print(f"Durée min          : {stats['dur_min']:.2f} s")
    print(f"Durée max          : {stats['dur_max']:.2f} s")
    print("==============================================================================")

# ============================================================
# MAIN
# ============================================================

def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Analyse FULL PRO des trades enregistrés")
    parser.add_argument("--inst", help="Filtrer par instrument (ex: BTCUSDT)", required=False)
    args = parser.parse_args()

    rows = load_records(inst=args.inst)
    if not rows:
        print("Aucun trade recordé.")
        return

    display_table(rows)

    stats = compute_stats(rows)
    display_stats(stats)

    analyse_reason(rows)
    analyse_side(rows)
    analyse_inst(rows)
    analyse_hours(rows)
    analyse_durations(rows)
    analyse_duration_by_reason(rows)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/analyse_recorder.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
Analyse complète des trades déjà enregistrés dans recorder.db.
Version stable V211.
"""

import sqlite3
from statistics import mean, median
import time

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project"
DB_R = f"{ROOT}/data/recorder.db"

def conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_R)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return c

def load():
    c = conn()
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT
            uid,
            instId,
            side,
            reason_signal,
            reason_close,
            price_signal,
            atr_signal,
            score_A,
            score_B,
            ts_open,
            ts_close,
            entry,
            price_close,
            sl_init,
            tp_init,
            sl_be,
            sl_trail,
            tp_dyn,
            price_to_close,
            pnl
        FROM v_trades_analyse;
    """).fetchall()

    trades = []
    for r in rows:
        trades.append({
            "uid": r[0],
            "instId": r[1],
            "side": r[2],
            "pattern": r[3],
            "reason_close": r[4],
            "price_signal": r[5],
            "atr": r[6],
            "score_A": r[7],
            "score_B": r[8],
            "ts_open": r[9],
            "ts_close": r[10],
            "entry": r[11],
            "price_close": r[12],
            "sl_init": r[13],
            "tp_init": r[14],
            "sl_be": r[15],
            "sl_trail": r[16],
            "tp_dyn": r[17],
            "price_to_close": r[18],
            "pnl": r[19]
        })
    return trades

def stats(lst):
    pnls = [t["pnl"] for t in lst]
    wins = [p for p in pnls if p > 0]
    losses = [p for p in pnls if p <= 0]

    return {
        "count": len(lst),
        "winrate": len(wins) / len(lst) * 100 if lst else 0,
        "avg_pnl": mean(pnls) if pnls else 0,
        "median_pnl": median(pnls) if pnls else 0,
        "max_win": max(pnls) if pnls else 0,
        "max_loss": min(pnls) if pnls else 0,
        "profit_factor": abs(sum(wins)) / abs(sum(losses)) if wins and losses else None,
    }

def group(trades, key):
    out = {}
    for t in trades:
        k = t[key]
        out.setdefault(k, []).append(t)
    return out

def print_section(title):
    print("\n" + "="*70)
    print(title)
    print("="*70)

def show(name, d):
    print("\n>>>", name)
    for k, v in d.items():
        print(f"  {k:15s}: {v}")

def main():
    trades = load()
    if not trades:
        print("Aucun trade recorded.")
        return

    print_section("STATISTIQUES GLOBALES")
    show("GLOBAL", stats(trades))

    print_section("PAR INSTRUMENT")
    for inst, lst in group(trades, "instId").items():
        show(inst, stats(lst))

    print_section("PAR PATTERN")
    for pat, lst in group(trades, "pattern").items():
        show(pat, stats(lst))

    print_section("PAR SIDE")
    for side, lst in group(trades, "side").items():
        show(side, stats(lst))

    print_section("PAR HEURE D'OUVERTURE")
    for h, lst in group(trades, "ts_open").items():
        hour = time.strftime("%Hh", time.localtime(h/1000))
        show(hour, stats(lst))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/analytics.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, time, traceback

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/analytics.db"
DB_R = "/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db"

def conn(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return c

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# FETCH RECORDED TRADES (base historique)
# -------------------------------------------------------------------
def load_trades():
    c = conn(DB_R)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT
            instId,
            side,
            reason,
            ctx,
            score_A,
            score_B,
            atr_signal,
            pnl_net,
            ts_signal
        FROM trades_recorded
        WHERE status = 'recorded';
    """).fetchall()

    trades = []
    for r in rows:
        inst, side, reason, ctx_dir, scoreA, scoreB, atr, pnl, ts = r

        # Buckets
        scoreC_bucket = (
            'strong' if scoreA >= 0.70 else
            'weak' if scoreA <= 0.30 else
            'mid'
        )

        scoreS_bucket = (
            'strong' if scoreB >= 0.70 else
            'weak' if scoreB <= 0.30 else
            'mid'
        )

        if atr <= 0.5:
            atr_bucket = 'low'
        elif atr <= 1.5:
            atr_bucket = 'mid'
        else:
            atr_bucket = 'high'

        # hour + weekday
        hour = int((ts // 1000) % 86400 // 3600)
        if 2 <= hour <= 10:
            hour_bucket = 1
        elif 11 <= hour <= 16:
            hour_bucket = 2
        elif 17 <= hour <= 22:
            hour_bucket = 3
        else:
            hour_bucket = 4

        weekday = int((ts // 1000) % (7*86400) // 86400)
        weekday_bucket = (
            'weekend' if weekday in (5,6) else
            'fri' if weekday == 4 else
            'mon' if weekday == 0 else
            'tue_thu'
        )

        trades.append((
            inst, side, reason, ctx_dir,
            scoreC_bucket, scoreS_bucket,
            atr_bucket, pnl, hour_bucket,
            weekday_bucket
        ))

    return trades

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# COMPUTE SCORES
# -------------------------------------------------------------------
def compute_scores(trades):
    agg = {}

    for inst, side, reason, ctx, cB, sB, atrB, pnl, hB, wdB in trades:
        key = (inst, side, reason, ctx, cB, sB, atrB, hB, wdB)

        if key not in agg:
            agg[key] = {"wins": 0, "count": 0, "pnl_sum": 0}

        agg[key]["count"] += 1
        agg[key]["pnl_sum"] += pnl
        if pnl > 0:
            agg[key]["wins"] += 1

    rows = []
    ts_now = int(time.time() * 1000)

    for key, stats in agg.items():
        inst, side, reason, ctx, cB, sB, atrB, hB, wdB = key
        win_rate = stats["wins"] / stats["count"]
        pnl_avg  = stats["pnl_sum"] / stats["count"]

        score_H = 0.5 * win_rate + 0.5 * max(0, pnl_avg)
        score_H = max(0, min(score_H, 1))

        # booster directionnel simple
        if ctx == 'bullish' and side == 'buy':
            score_dir = 1.05
        elif ctx == 'bearish' and side == 'sell':
            score_dir = 1.05
        else:
            score_dir = 0.95

        score_H_final = max(0, min(score_H * score_dir, 1))

        rows.append((
            inst, side, reason,
            ctx, cB, sB,
            atrB, None, hB, wdB,
            win_rate, pnl_avg,
            score_H, score_H_final,
            ts_now
        ))

    return rows

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# SAVE TO DB
# -------------------------------------------------------------------
def save(rows):
    c = conn(DB_A)
    c.executemany("""
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO historical_scores (
            instId, side, reason,
            ctx_dir, score_C_bucket, score_S_bucket,
            atr_bucket, of_bucket,
            hour_bucket, weekday_bucket,
            win_rate, pnl_avg,
            score_H, score_H_final,
            ts_updated
        )
        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?);
    """, rows)

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# MAIN
# -------------------------------------------------------------------
def main():
    try:
        trades = load_trades()
        rows = compute_scores(trades)
        save(rows)
        print(f"OK analytics: {len(rows)} rows updated")
    except Exception as e:
        print("ERR analytics", e, traceback.format_exc())

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/analytics_historical.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, time
from statistics import mean

DB_REC = "/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db"
DB_A   = "/opt/scalp/project/data/analytics.db"

def conn(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=3, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return c

# --------------------------------------------------------------------
# BUCKETS
# --------------------------------------------------------------------
def bucket_ctx(ctx, score_A):
    if ctx in ("bullish", "bearish", "flat"):
        return ctx
    return "unknown"

def bucket_hour(ts_open):
    from datetime import datetime
    h = datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts_open/1000).hour
    if 0 <= h < 6:   return 0
    if 6 <= h < 12:  return 1
    if 12 <= h < 18: return 2
    return 3

def bucket_weekday(ts_open):
    from datetime import datetime
    wd = datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts_open/1000).weekday()
    if wd in (1,2,3): return "tue_thu"
    if wd == 4:       return "fri"
    if wd in (5,6):   return "weekend"
    return "mon"

def bucket_atr(atr_value):
    if atr_value is None: return "unknown"
    if atr_value < 0.005: return "low"
    if atr_value < 0.015: return "mid"
    return "high"

def bucket_of(of_strength):
    if of_strength is None: return "unknown"
    if of_strength < 0.33:  return "weak"
    if of_strength < 0.66:  return "mid"
    return "strong"

# --------------------------------------------------------------------
# MAIN : CALCUL H
# --------------------------------------------------------------------
def compute_historical():
    cR = conn(DB_REC)
    cA = conn(DB_A)

    rows = cR.execute("""
        SELECT
            instId, side, reason,
            pnl_net, pnl_pct,
            ctx, score_A,
            ts_open,
            atr_signal
        FROM trades_recorded
        WHERE status='recorded'
    """).fetchall()

    groups = {}
    for instId, side, reason, pnl_net, pnl_pct, ctx, score_A, ts_open, atr_signal in rows:
        key = (instId, side, reason)
        if key not in groups:
            groups[key] = {
                "pnls": [],
                "pct": [],
                "ctx": [],
                "ts": [],
                "atr": []
            }
        groups[key]["pnls"].append(pnl_net)
        groups[key]["pct"].append(pnl_pct)
        groups[key]["ctx"].append((ctx, score_A))
        groups[key]["ts"].append(ts_open)
        groups[key]["atr"].append(atr_signal)

    cA.execute("DELETE FROM historical_scores;")

    now = int(time.time()*1000)

    for (instId, side, reason), g in groups.items():

        wins = [p for p in g["pnls"] if p > 0]
        win_rate = len(wins) / len(g["pnls"])

        pnl_avg = mean(g["pct"]) if g["pct"] else 0.0

        score_H = 0.5*win_rate + 0.5*(pnl_avg/0.01)
        if score_H < 0: score_H = 0
        if score_H > 1: score_H = 1

        ctx, scoreA = g["ctx"][-1]
        ctx_dir = bucket_ctx(ctx, scoreA)

        ts_ref = g["ts"][-1]
        hour_b = bucket_hour(ts_ref)
        wd_b   = bucket_weekday(ts_ref)

        atr_ref = g["atr"][-1]
        atr_b = bucket_atr(atr_ref)

        of_b = "unknown"

        cA.execute("""
            INSERT INTO historical_scores(
                instId, side, reason,
                win_rate, pnl_avg, score_H,
                ctx_dir, hour_bucket, weekday_bucket,
                atr_bucket, of_bucket,
                ts_updated
            ) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """, (
            instId, side, reason,
            win_rate, pnl_avg, score_H,
            ctx_dir, hour_b, wd_b,
            atr_b, of_b,
            now
        ))

    cA.commit()
    cA.close()
    cR.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    compute_historical()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/budget.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    print(f"[BUDGET] Event logged: {instId} → {event}")

def main():
    while True:
        print("[BUDGET] Updating exposure / allocation")
        bus_notify("ALL", "BUDGET_UPDATED")
        time.sleep(20)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/budget_updater.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, logging, sys
from pathlib import Path

DB_BUDGET  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db")
DB_OPENER  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db")
DB_CLOSER  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db")
DB_REC     = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db")
LOG        = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/budget.log"

# -----------------------------------------------------
def setup_logging():
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.INFO,
        format="%(asctime)s BUDGET %(levelname)s %(message)s",
        handlers=[logging.FileHandler(LOG), logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)],
        force=True,
    )

# -----------------------------------------------------
def connect(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return c

# -----------------------------------------------------
def get_margin_engaged(con_o):
    """Somme de la marge estimée sur les positions ouvertes/pending."""
    try:
        res = con_o.execute("""
            SELECT SUM(entry * qty / leverage)
            FROM trades_open_init
            WHERE status IN ('pending','open');
        """).fetchone()[0]
        return round(res or 0.0, 4)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def get_pnl_real(con_r):
    """Somme du PnL réalisé total depuis l’historique."""
    try:
        res = con_r.execute("SELECT SUM(pnl_net) FROM trades_recorded;").fetchone()[0]
        if res is None:
            res = con_r.execute("SELECT SUM(pnl) FROM trades_recorded;").fetchone()[0]
        return round(res or 0.0, 4)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def get_capital_initial(con_b):
    """Capital initial du budget (si non encore présent, crée 1000 USDT)."""
    con_b.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS budget_state(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id=1),
            balance REAL DEFAULT 1000.0,
            margin REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            pnl_real REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            ts_update INTEGER
        );
    """)
    con_b.commit()
    row = con_b.execute("SELECT balance FROM budget_state WHERE id=1;").fetchone()
    if not row:
        con_b.execute("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO budget_state(id,balance,margin,pnl_real,ts_update) VALUES (1,1000.0,0.0,0.0,strftime('%s','now'));")
        con_b.commit()
        return 1000.0
    return float(row[0])

# -----------------------------------------------------
def update_budget():
    con_b = connect(DB_BUDGET)
    con_o = connect(DB_OPENER)
    con_r = connect(DB_REC)

    capital = get_capital_initial(con_b)
    margin  = get_margin_engaged(con_o)
    pnl_real = get_pnl_real(con_r)

    new_balance = capital + pnl_real
    ts_now = int(time.time())

    con_b.execute("""
        UPDATE budget_state
        SET balance=?, margin=?, pnl_real=?, ts_update=?
        WHERE id=1;
    """, (new_balance, margin, pnl_real, ts_now))
    con_b.commit()

    con_b.execute("""
        CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_budget_overview AS
        SELECT
            ROUND(balance,4) AS balance,
            ROUND(margin,4)  AS margin,
            ROUND(pnl_real,4) AS pnl_real,
            datetime(ts_update,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
        FROM budget_state;
    """)
    con_b.commit()

    con_b.close(); con_o.close(); con_r.close()
    logging.info(f"MAJ budget → balance={new_balance:.2f} margin={margin:.2f} pnl_real={pnl_real:.2f}")

# -----------------------------------------------------
def main(_):
    setup_logging()
    logging.info("Budget updater started ✓")
    try:
        update_budget()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.exception(f"Erreur mise à jour budget: {e}")
        raise SystemExit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv[1:]))

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/check_recorder.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
CHECK_RECORDER v211
Outil de validation complet du module RECORDER.

Vérifie :
- Colonnes physiques dans recorder.trades_record
- Colonnes exposées par gest.v_for_recorder
- Compatibilité réelle entre les deux
- Colonnes manquantes / inutilisées
- Données incohérentes
"""

import sqlite3
import time

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project"
DB_G = f"{ROOT}/data/gest.db"
DB_R = f"{ROOT}/data/recorder.db"

line = lambda: print("=" * 70)

def conn(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return c


# --------------------------------------------------------------
# Inspection des colonnes
# --------------------------------------------------------------
def list_columns(conn, table_or_view):
    rows = conn.execute(f"PRAGMA table_info({table_or_view});").fetchall()
    return [r[1] for r in rows]  # r[1] = column name


def check_columns():
    print("\n")
    line()
    print("CHECK DES COLONNES (GEST vs RECORDER)")
    line()

    cG = conn(DB_G)
    cR = conn(DB_R)

    cols_view = list_columns(cG, "v_for_recorder")
    cols_rec = list_columns(cR, "trades_record")

    print("\nColonnes dans gest.v_for_recorder :")
    for c in cols_view:
        print("  -", c)

    print("\nColonnes dans recorder.trades_record :")
    for c in cols_rec:
        print("  -", c)

    line()
    print("INTERSECTION (colonnes compatibles) :")
    common = [c for c in cols_view if c in cols_rec]
    for c in common:
        print("  *", c)

    line()
    print("Colonnes MANQUANTES dans recorder.trades_record :")
    missing = [c for c in cols_view if c not in cols_rec]
    if missing:
        for c in missing:
            print("  -", c)
    else:
        print("  OK : aucune colonne manquante.")

    line()
    print("Colonnes INUTILES dans recorder.trades_record (non envoyées par gest) :")
    extra = [c for c in cols_rec if c not in cols_view]
    if extra:
        for c in extra:
            print("  -", c)
    else:
        print("  OK : aucune colonne inutile.")

    line()
    return common, missing, extra


# --------------------------------------------------------------
# Vérification des données
# --------------------------------------------------------------
def check_data():
    print("\n")
    line()
    print("CHECK DU CONTENU DES DONNÉES RECORDED")
    line()

    cR = conn(DB_R)

    # Nombre total
    n = cR.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trades_record;").fetchone()[0]
    print(f"\nNombre total de trades recorded : {n}")

    if n == 0:
        print("AUCUNE donnée à analyser — recorder ne reçoit rien.")
        return

    # Inspecter un échantillon
    rows = cR.execute("SELECT * FROM trades_record LIMIT 5;").fetchall()
    cols = list_columns(cR, "trades_record")

    print("\nAperçu des 5 premières lignes :\n")
    for row in rows:
        for i, v in enumerate(row):
            print(f"{cols[i]:20s} = {v}")
        print("-" * 40)

    # Vérifier timestamps incohérents
    rows_ts = cR.execute("""
        SELECT uid, ts_open, ts_close
        FROM trades_record
        WHERE ts_close < ts_open AND ts_close > 0;
    """).fetchall()

    line()
    print("CHECK TIMESTAMPS : ts_close < ts_open :")
    if rows_ts:
        for r in rows_ts:
            print("  INCOHERENT :", r)
    else:
        print("  OK : aucune incohérence temporelle.")

    # Vérifier pnl nuls
    rows_pnl = cR.execute("""
        SELECT uid, pnl FROM trades_record WHERE pnl = 0;
    """).fetchall()

    line()
    print("CHECK PNL = 0 :")
    print(f"  Nombre de trades avec pnl=0 : {len(rows_pnl)}")

    line()


# --------------------------------------------------------------
# Programme principal
# --------------------------------------------------------------
def main():
    print("CHECK_RECORDER v211 — Analyse complète\n")

    common, missing, extra = check_columns()
    check_data()

    line()
    print("SYNTHÈSE :")

    if missing:
        print("\n*** DES COLONNES MANQUENT DANS recorder.trades_record ***")
        print("Le recorder ne peut PAS fonctionner correctement tant que ces colonnes ne sont pas ajoutées.")
        print("Colonnes manquantes :", missing)
    else:
        print("\nOK : Toutes les colonnes nécessaires sont présentes.")

    if extra:
        print("\nNote : Certaines colonnes sont présentes dans recorder mais jamais alimentées par gest.")
        print("Colonnes inutilisées :", extra)

    print("\nAnalyse terminée.")
    line()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/closer.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3
import time
import logging
from pathlib import Path

ROOT = Path("/opt/scalp/project")
DB_GEST      = ROOT / "data/gest.db"
DB_CLOSER    = ROOT / "data/closer.db"
DB_ORDERFLOW = ROOT / "data/orderflow.db"

LOG = ROOT / "logs/closer.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=str(LOG),
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s CLOSER %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)

###############################################################################
# UTILITAIRES
###############################################################################

def now_ms():
    return int(time.time() * 1000)

def fetch_bidask(instId_raw):
    inst = instId_raw.replace("/", "")
    try:
        c = sqlite3.connect(DB_ORDERFLOW, timeout=1)
        r = c.execute("""
            SELECT best_bid, best_ask
            FROM books1
            WHERE instId = ?
            ORDER BY ts_ms DESC
            LIMIT 1;
        """, (inst,)).fetchone()
        return r if r else (None, None)
    except:
        return (None, None)

def exec_price(instId, side):
    bid, ask = fetch_bidask(instId)
    if bid is None or ask is None:
        return None
    return (ask if side == "buy" else bid)

###############################################################################
# LECTURE GEST
###############################################################################

def fetch_to_close():
    """
    Sélection depuis gest : uniquement les trades marqués 'to_close'.
    gest fournit : uid, instId, side, entry, qty, lev, sl/trail/dyn, etc.
    """
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_GEST)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT
            uid,
            instId,
            side,
            entry,
            qty,
            lev,
            margin,
            sl_be,
            sl_trail,
            tp_dyn,
            price_to_close,
            ts_open,
            ts_follow,
            ts_signal,
            atr_signal
        FROM v_gest
        WHERE status='to_close'
        ORDER BY ts_follow ASC;
    """).fetchall()
    return rows

###############################################################################
# ENREGISTREMENT
###############################################################################

def store_close(uid, instId, side, price, pnl, pnl_pct, fee, reason_close):
    ts = now_ms()
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_CLOSER)
    conn.execute("""
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO closer(
            uid, instId, side,
            ts_close, price_exec_close,
            pnl, pnl_pct, fee,
            reason_close,
            ts_status_update
        )
        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
    """, (
        uid, instId, side,
        ts, price,
        pnl, pnl_pct, fee,
        reason_close,
        ts
    ))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

###############################################################################
# CALCULS INSTITUTIONNELS
###############################################################################

def compute_pnl(entry, exec_price, qty, side):
    if side == "buy":
        return (exec_price - entry) * qty
    else:
        return (entry - exec_price) * qty

def compute_pnl_pct(pnl, margin):
    if margin <= 0:
        return 0.0
    return pnl / margin

def compute_fee(exec_price, qty, fee_rate=0.0006):
    """Taker local minimal."""
    return exec_price * qty * fee_rate

###############################################################################
# MAIN LOOP
###############################################################################

def main():
    logging.info("[START] closer running")

    while True:
        try:
            rows = fetch_to_close()

            for (uid, instId, side, entry, qty, lev, margin,
                 sl_be, sl_trail, tp_dyn,
                 price_to_close, ts_open, ts_follow,
                 ts_signal, atr_signal) in rows:

                price = exec_price(instId, side)
                if price is None:
                    continue

                pnl = compute_pnl(entry, price, qty, side)
                pnl_pct = compute_pnl_pct(pnl, margin)
                fee = compute_fee(price, qty)

                # Détermination propre de reason_close
                if sl_be and ((side == "buy" and price <= sl_be) or (side == "sell" and price >= sl_be)):
                    reason = "BE"
                elif sl_trail and ((side == "buy" and price <= sl_trail) or (side == "sell" and price >= sl_trail)):
                    reason = "TRAIL"
                elif tp_dyn and ((side == "buy" and price >= tp_dyn) or (side == "sell" and price <= tp_dyn)):
                    reason = "TP"
                else:
                    reason = "SYS"

                store_close(uid, instId, side, price, pnl, pnl_pct, fee, reason)

                logging.info(f"[CLOSE] {uid} {instId} {side} price={price} pnl={pnl:.4f} reason={reason}")

        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"[ERR] closer loop {e}")

        time.sleep(0.5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/closer_finalize.py -----
import sqlite3, time, logging

DB_FOLLOW = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_CLOSER = "/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
DB_REC = "/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db"
DB_BUDGET = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"
DB_TICKS = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s CLOSER FIX %(levelname)s %(message)s")

def get_last_price(instId):
    """Récupère le dernier prix connu depuis t.db"""
    try:
        with sqlite3.connect(DB_TICKS) as ct:
            cur = ct.cursor()
            cur.execute("SELECT lastPr FROM v_ticks_latest WHERE instId=? LIMIT 1;", (instId,))
            row = cur.fetchone()
            return float(row[0]) if row else None
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"{instId}: erreur lecture ticks → {e}")
        return None

def finalize_closures():
    con_f = sqlite3.connect(DB_FOLLOW)
    con_c = sqlite3.connect(DB_CLOSER)
    con_r = sqlite3.connect(DB_REC)
    con_b = sqlite3.connect(DB_BUDGET)

    cur_f = con_f.cursor()
    cur_c = con_c.cursor()
    cur_r = con_r.cursor()
    cur_b = con_b.cursor()

    rows = cur_f.execute("""
        SELECT instId, side, entry, last, qty, reason_close,
               score_U, score_A, score_B, ts_open, ts_update
        FROM trades_follow
        WHERE status='to_close'
    """).fetchall()

    if not rows:
        logging.info("Aucune position à finaliser.")
        return

    for instId, side, entry, last, qty, reason, sU, sA, sB, ts_open, ts_close in rows:
        if last is None:
            last = get_last_price(instId)
            if last is None:
                last = entry
                logging.warning(f"{instId}: aucun prix disponible → fallback entry={entry}")
            else:
                logging.info(f"{instId}: récupéré last depuis ticks = {last}")

        pnl = round((last - entry) * qty * (1 if side == 'buy' else -1), 6)
        logging.info(f"→ CLOSE {instId} {side} pnl={pnl} reason={reason}")

        cur_c.execute("""
            INSERT INTO positions_closed(instId,side,entry,exit,qty,pnl,sl,tp,ts_open,ts_close,reason_exit,score_U,score_A,score_B)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """, (instId,side,entry,last,qty,pnl,0,0,ts_open,ts_close,reason,sU,sA,sB))

        cur_r.execute("""
            INSERT INTO trades_recorded(instId,side,entry,exit,pnl,reason_exit,ts_open,ts_close,score_U,score_A,score_B)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """, (instId,side,entry,last,pnl,reason,ts_open,ts_close,sU,sA,sB))

        cur_b.execute("""
            INSERT INTO ledger(src,instId,type,amount,ts)
            VALUES ('closer',?, 'pnl_real', ?, strftime('%s','now')*1000)
        """, (instId, pnl))

        cur_f.execute("UPDATE trades_follow SET status='closed' WHERE instId=?;", (instId,))

    con_c.commit()
    con_r.commit()
    con_b.commit()
    con_f.commit()
    logging.info(f"✓ {len(rows)} clôture(s) finalisée(s).")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    finalize_closures()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/detectors/atr.py -----
def detect_atr_triggers(feats):
    out = []
    atrs = feats["atr"]
    for inst, rows in atrs.items():
        if len(rows) < 10:
            continue
        last_ts, last_atr = rows[-1]
        m = sum(v for _, v in rows[-10:]) / 10

        ctx = feats["ctx"].get(inst, {"ctx":"flat","score_C":0})

        if last_atr > 1.5 * m:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "buy",
                "reason": "ATR_EXPANSION",
                "type_signal": "ATR",
                "score_C": abs(ctx["score_C"]),
                "score_S": 0.4,
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 1,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": last_ts,
                "price_signal": None,
                "atr_signal": last_atr,
            })

        if last_atr < 0.7 * m:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "sell",
                "reason": "ATR_CONTRACTION",
                "type_signal": "ATR",
                "score_C": abs(ctx["score_C"]),
                "score_S": 0.4,
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 0.2,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": last_ts,
                "price_signal": None,
                "atr_signal": last_atr,
            })

    return out

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/detectors/breakout.py -----
def detect(instId, candles, orderflow, ctx):
    signals = []
    if len(candles) < 5:
        return signals

    c1 = candles[-1]
    high_last = c1["high"]
    low_last = c1["low"]

    prev_highs = [c["high"] for c in candles[-5:-1]]
    prev_lows  = [c["low"] for c in candles[-5:-1]]

    if high_last > max(prev_highs):
        signals.append({
            "instId": instId,
            "side": "buy",
            "type_signal": "BREAKOUT",
            "reason": "HH_break",
            "price_signal": high_last
        })

    if low_last < min(prev_lows):
        signals.append({
            "instId": instId,
            "side": "sell",
            "type_signal": "BREAKOUT",
            "reason": "LL_break",
            "price_signal": low_last
        })

    return signals

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/detectors/exhaustion.py -----
def detect_exhaustion(feats):
    out = []
    prices = feats["price"]
    atrs = feats["atr"]

    for inst, rows in prices.items():
        if inst not in atrs:
            continue
        if len(rows) < 3 or len(atrs[inst]) < 1:
            continue

        last_ts, last_px = rows[-1]
        atr = atrs[inst][-1][1]

        if atr <= 0:
            continue

        ctx = feats["ctx"].get(inst, {"ctx":"flat","score_C":0})

        prev_ts, prev_px = rows[-2]
        jump = last_px - prev_px

        if jump > 1.8 * atr:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "sell",
                "reason": "EXHAUSTION_UP",
                "type_signal": "EXHAUSTION",
                "score_C": abs(ctx["score_C"]),
                "score_S": min(1, jump / atr),
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 1.0,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": last_ts,
                "price_signal": last_px,
                "atr_signal": atr,
            })

        if -jump > 1.8 * atr:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "buy",
                "reason": "EXHAUSTION_DOWN",
                "type_signal": "EXHAUSTION",
                "score_C": abs(ctx["score_C"]),
                "score_S": min(1, abs(jump) / atr),
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 1.0,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": last_ts,
                "price_signal": last_px,
                "atr_signal": atr,
            })
    return out

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/detectors/momentum.py -----
def detect_momentum(feats):
    out = []
    prices = feats["price"]
    for inst, rows in prices.items():
        if len(rows) < 6:
            continue
        last_ts, last_px = rows[-1]
        px_5 = rows[-6][1]
        slope = last_px - px_5

        ctx = feats["ctx"].get(inst, {"ctx":"flat","score_C":0})
        score_C = abs(ctx["score_C"])

        if slope > 0:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "buy",
                "reason": "MOMENTUM_UP",
                "type_signal": "MOMENTUM",
                "score_C": score_C,
                "score_S": min(1, slope * 5),
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 0.5,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": last_ts,
                "price_signal": last_px,
                "atr_signal": 0,
            })
        elif slope < 0:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "sell",
                "reason": "MOMENTUM_DOWN",
                "type_signal": "MOMENTUM",
                "score_C": score_C,
                "score_S": min(1, abs(slope) * 5),
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 0.5,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": last_ts,
                "price_signal": last_px,
                "atr_signal": 0,
            })
    return out

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/detectors/orderflow.py -----
def detect_orderflow_triggers(feats):
    out = []
    ofs = feats["of"]
    for inst, rows in ofs.items():
        if len(rows) < 1:
            continue
        ts, bb, ba, bs, asz = rows[-1]

        if bb is None or ba is None or bs is None or asz is None:
            continue

        imbalance = (bs - asz) / max(1, bs + asz)

        ctx = feats["ctx"].get(inst, {"ctx":"flat","score_C":0})
        score_C = abs(ctx["score_C"])

        if imbalance > 0.4:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "buy",
                "reason": "ORDERFLOW_IMBALANCE_BUY",
                "type_signal": "ORDERFLOW",
                "score_C": score_C,
                "score_S": 0.3 + imbalance,
                "score_OF": imbalance,
                "score_ATR": 0.5,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": ts,
                "price_signal": bb,
                "atr_signal": None
            })

        if imbalance < -0.4:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "sell",
                "reason": "ORDERFLOW_IMBALANCE_SELL",
                "type_signal": "ORDERFLOW",
                "score_C": score_C,
                "score_S": 0.3 + abs(imbalance),
                "score_OF": abs(imbalance),
                "score_ATR": 0.5,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": ts,
                "price_signal": ba,
                "atr_signal": None
            })
    return out

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/detectors/reversal.py -----
def detect_reversal(feats):
    out = []
    prices = feats["price"]
    for inst, rows in prices.items():
        if len(rows) < 4:
            continue

        ts1, p1 = rows[-1]
        ts2, p2 = rows[-2]
        ts3, p3 = rows[-3]

        ctx = feats["ctx"].get(inst, {"ctx":"flat","score_C":0})

        if p3 < p2 > p1:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "sell",
                "reason": "REVERSAL_TOP",
                "type_signal": "REVERSAL",
                "score_C": abs(ctx["score_C"]),
                "score_S": 0.5,
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 0.5,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": ts1,
                "price_signal": p1,
                "atr_signal": 0
            })

        if p3 > p2 < p1:
            out.append({
                "instId": inst,
                "side": "buy",
                "reason": "REVERSAL_BOTTOM",
                "type_signal": "REVERSAL",
                "score_C": abs(ctx["score_C"]),
                "score_S": 0.5,
                "score_OF": 0,
                "score_ATR": 0.5,
                "score_T": 0,
                "ctx": ctx["ctx"],
                "ts_signal": ts1,
                "price_signal": p1,
                "atr_signal": 0
            })
    return out

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/feature_loader.py -----
import sqlite3, time

DB_T = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
DB_OF = "/opt/scalp/project/data/orderflow.db"
DB_CTX = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ctx.db"

def load_features():
    return {
        "price": load_price(),
        "atr": load_atr(),
        "of": load_orderflow(),
        "ctx": load_ctx()
    }

def load_price():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_T)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT instId, ts, price
        FROM ticks
        WHERE ts > ?
    """, (int(time.time()*1000)-5000,)).fetchall()
    data = {}
    for inst, ts, px in rows:
        data.setdefault(inst, []).append((ts, px))
    return data

def load_atr():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_T)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT instId, ts, atr
        FROM atr
        WHERE ts > ?
    """, (int(time.time()*1000)-60000,)).fetchall()
    data = {}
    for inst, ts, v in rows:
        data.setdefault(inst, []).append((ts, v))
    return data

def load_orderflow():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_OF)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT instId, ts_ms, best_bid, best_ask, bid_size, ask_size
        FROM books1
        WHERE ts_ms > ?
    """, (int(time.time()*1000)-5000,)).fetchall()
    data = {}
    for inst, ts, bb, ba, bs, asz in rows:
        data.setdefault(inst, []).append((ts, bb, ba, bs, asz))
    return data

def load_ctx():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB_CTX)
    rows = c.execute("""
        SELECT instId, ctx, score_final
        FROM v_ctx_latest
    """).fetchall()
    return {r[0]: {"ctx": r[1], "score_C": r[2]} for r in rows}

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/fetch_contracts.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import requests
import sqlite3
import time

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/contracts.db"

# ============================================================
# UTIL : parse float safe
# ============================================================

def parse_float(x, default=0.0):
    """
    Convertit proprement n'importe quelle valeur Bitget en float.
    - '', None  -> default
    - '123.45'  -> 123.45
    """
    if x is None:
        return default
    if isinstance(x, (int, float)):
        return float(x)
    x = str(x).strip()
    if x == "":
        return default
    try:
        return float(x)
    except:
        return default

# ============================================================
# TABLE SCHEMA
# ============================================================

schema = """
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contracts (
    symbol TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    baseCoin TEXT,
    quoteCoin TEXT,
    minTradeNum REAL,
    minTradeUSDT REAL,
    pricePlace INTEGER,
    volumePlace INTEGER,
    sizeMultiplier REAL,
    minLever INTEGER,
    maxLever INTEGER,
    makerFee REAL,
    takerFee REAL,
    maxOrderQty REAL,
    maxMarketOrderQty REAL,
    symbolStatus TEXT,
    last_update INTEGER
);
"""

# ============================================================
# FETCH FROM BITGET
# ============================================================

URL = "https://api.bitget.com/api/v2/mix/market/contracts?productType=usdt-futures"

def fetch():
    r = requests.get(URL, timeout=5)
    r.raise_for_status()
    data = r.json()
    return data["data"]

# ============================================================
# SAVE TO DB
# ============================================================

def save(rows):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    conn.execute(schema)

    query = """
    INSERT OR REPLACE INTO contracts (
        symbol, baseCoin, quoteCoin,
        minTradeNum, minTradeUSDT,
        pricePlace, volumePlace, sizeMultiplier,
        minLever, maxLever,
        makerFee, takerFee,
        maxOrderQty, maxMarketOrderQty,
        symbolStatus, last_update
    )
    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?);
    """

    now = int(time.time() * 1000)

    for d in rows:
        conn.execute(query, (
            d.get("symbol"),
            d.get("baseCoin"),
            d.get("quoteCoin"),

            parse_float(d.get("minTradeNum")),
            parse_float(d.get("minTradeUSDT")),

            int(parse_float(d.get("pricePlace"))),
            int(parse_float(d.get("volumePlace"))),
            parse_float(d.get("sizeMultiplier")),

            int(parse_float(d.get("minLever"), 1)),
            int(parse_float(d.get("maxLever"), 1)),

            parse_float(d.get("makerFeeRate")),
            parse_float(d.get("takerFeeRate")),

            parse_float(d.get("maxOrderQty")),
            parse_float(d.get("maxMarketOrderQty")),

            d.get("symbolStatus", "unknown"),
            now
        ))

    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

# ============================================================
# MAIN
# ============================================================

def main():
    rows = fetch()
    save(rows)
    print(f"Saved {len(rows)} contracts into contracts.db")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
