-- VIEWS --
v_atr_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_atr_bucket AS
SELECT
    instId,
    CASE
        WHEN atr_signal <= 0.5 THEN 'low'
        WHEN atr_signal <= 1.5 THEN 'mid'
        ELSE 'high'
    END AS atr_bucket
FROM trades_recorded
v_ctx_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_ctx_bucket AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ctx AS ctx_dir,
    CASE
        WHEN score_A >= 0.70 THEN 'strong'
        WHEN score_A <= 0.30 THEN 'weak'
        ELSE 'mid'
    END AS score_C_bucket
FROM ctx_A
v_ctx_latest|CREATE VIEW v_ctx_latest AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ctx,
    score_A AS score_C,
    ts_updated
FROM ctx_A
WHERE ts_updated = (
    SELECT MAX(ts_updated) FROM ctx_A c2 WHERE c2.instId = ctx_A.instId
)
v_historical|CREATE VIEW v_historical AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    type_signal,
    ctx,
    score_C,
    score_S,
    score_OF,
    atr_bucket,
    win_rate,
    pnl_avg,
    score_H,
    score_H AS score_H_final,
    ts_updated
FROM historical_scores
ORDER BY ts_updated DESC
v_orderflow_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_orderflow_bucket AS
SELECT
    instId,
    CASE
        WHEN imbalance >= 0.20 THEN 'strong_buy'
        WHEN imbalance <= -0.20 THEN 'strong_sell'
        ELSE 'neutral'
    END AS of_bucket
FROM v_orderflow_features
v_score_H|CREATE VIEW v_score_H AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    ctx_dir,
    ctx_strength,
    signal_strength,
    day_bucket,
    hour_bucket,
    vol_bucket,
    of_bucket,
    total_trades,
    win_rate,
    avg_pnl,
    median_pnl,
    score_H,
    last_update
FROM historical_scores_v2
ORDER BY last_update DESC
v_scores_for_opener|CREATE VIEW v_scores_for_opener AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    ctx,
    scoreB_bucket,
    hour_bucket,
    score
FROM exposure_scores
v_signal_bucket|CREATE VIEW v_signal_bucket AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    score_B,
    CASE
        WHEN score_B >= 0.70 THEN 'strong'
        WHEN score_B <= 0.30 THEN 'weak'
        ELSE 'mid'
    END AS score_S_bucket
FROM signals_B
v_signal_timing|CREATE VIEW v_signal_timing AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    ts_signal,
    price_signal,
    peak_ts,
    peak_price,
    delta_t_ms,
    delta_price,
    delta_price_pct,
    score_T,
    ts_updated
FROM signal_timing
ORDER BY ts_updated DESC
v_timing|CREATE VIEW v_timing AS
SELECT *
FROM signal_timing
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC

-- INDEXES --

sqlite_autoindex_historical_scores_1|

sqlite_autoindex_signal_timing_1|

-- TABLES --

budget_state       ledger             v_budget_overview

[TABLE: balance]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|balance_usdt|REAL|1||0

[TABLE: bus_out]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|instId|TEXT|0||0
2|event|TEXT|0||0
3|ts|INTEGER|0|strftime('%s','now')*1000|0
4|ack|INTEGER|0|0|0
5|payload|TEXT|0||0
6|src|TEXT|0||0

[TABLE: v_balance]
0|balance_usdt|REAL|0||0

[TABLE: v_exposure]
0|instId|TEXT|0||0
1|margin||0||0
2|pnl_real||0||0

[TABLE: budget_state]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|balance|REAL|0|1000.0|0
2|margin|REAL|0|0.0|0
3|pnl_real|REAL|0|0.0|0
4|ts_update|INTEGER|0||0

[TABLE: ledger]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|src|TEXT|0||0
2|instId|TEXT|0||0
3|side|TEXT|0||0
4|type|TEXT|0||0
5|amount|REAL|0||0
6|ts|INTEGER|0|strftime('%s','now')*1000|0

[TABLE: v_budget_overview]
0|balance||0||0
1|margin||0||0
2|pnl_real||0||0
3|last_update||0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_balance|CREATE VIEW v_balance AS
SELECT balance_usdt
FROM balance
WHERE id = 1
v_budget_overview|CREATE VIEW v_budget_overview AS
SELECT
  ROUND(balance,6) AS balance,
  ROUND(margin,6)  AS margin,
  ROUND(pnl_real,6) AS pnl_real,
  datetime(ts_update,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update
FROM budget_state
v_exposure|CREATE VIEW v_exposure AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='margin' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS margin,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='pnl_real' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS pnl_real
FROM ledger
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY ABS(margin) DESC

-- INDEXES --
idx_bus_out_ack|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack)
idx_bus_out_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ts ON bus_out(ts)

-- TRIGGERS --

v_gest|CREATE VIEW v_gest AS
SELECT *
FROM gest
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
v_gest_status_count|CREATE VIEW v_gest_status_count AS
SELECT status, COUNT(*) AS n
FROM gest
GROUP BY status
ORDER BY
    CASE status
        WHEN 'new'       THEN 1
        WHEN 'opened'    THEN 2
        WHEN 'follow'    THEN 3
        WHEN 'to_close'  THEN 4
        WHEN 'closed'    THEN 5
        WHEN 'recorded'  THEN 6
        ELSE 99
    END

FROM ohlcv_15m

    ORDER BY ts DESC
    LIMIT 150
)

FROM ohlcv_30m

    LIMIT 150
)

0|key|TEXT|0||1
1|value|INTEGER|0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_orderflow_features|CREATE VIEW v_orderflow_features AS
WITH
    last_b1 AS (
        SELECT b.*
        FROM books1 b
        JOIN (
            SELECT instId, MAX(ts_ms) AS max_ts
            FROM books1
            WHERE ts_ms IS NOT NULL
            GROUP BY instId
        ) t
        ON b.instId = t.instId AND b.ts_ms = t.max_ts
    ),
    last_b5 AS (
        SELECT b.*
        FROM books5 b
        JOIN (
            SELECT instId, MAX(ts_ms) AS max_ts
            FROM books5
            WHERE ts_ms IS NOT NULL
            GROUP BY instId
        ) t
        ON b.instId = t.instId AND b.ts_ms = t.max_ts
    )

SELECT
    b1.instId,

    -- timestamps
    b1.ts_ms     AS ts_books1,
    b5.ts_ms     AS ts_books5,

    -- best prices
    b1.best_bid,
    b1.best_ask,

    -- micro sizes
    b1.bid_size,
    b1.ask_size,
    b1.imbalance,

    -- depth 5
    b5.mid,
    b5.spread,
    b5.bid1, b5.bid2, b5.bid3,
    b5.ask1, b5.ask2, b5.ask3,
    b5.wall_bid,
    b5.wall_ask,

    -- derived features
    (b5.wall_bid - b5.wall_ask) AS wall_diff,
    CASE WHEN (b5.wall_bid + b5.wall_ask) > 0
        THEN (b5.wall_bid - b5.wall_ask) * 1.0
             / (b5.wall_bid + b5.wall_ask)
        ELSE NULL
    END AS wall_ratio

FROM last_b1 b1
LEFT JOIN last_b5 b5 USING(instId)
ORDER BY b1.instId

-- INDEXES --
idx_b15_inst|CREATE INDEX idx_b15_inst ON books15(instId, ts_ms)
idx_b15_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_b15_ts ON books15(ts_ms)
sqlite_autoindex_meta_1|

v_for_gest|CREATE VIEW v_for_gest AS
SELECT
    s.trade_uid AS uid,
    s.instId,
    s.side,
    s.reason,
    s.ctx,
    s.score_A,
    s.score_B,
    s.price AS price_signal,
    s.atr   AS atr_signal,
    s.ts_signal
FROM signals s
JOIN (
    SELECT instId, MAX(ts_signal) AS max_ts
    FROM signals
    GROUP BY instId
) x ON x.instId = s.instId
   AND x.max_ts = s.ts_signal
ORDER BY s.ts_signal DESC

-- VIEWS --
v_atr|CREATE VIEW v_atr AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    -- fast ATR (10)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 10) AS atr_fast,

    -- slow ATR (30)
    (SELECT AVG(ABS(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr))
     FROM v_hist_ordered h2
     JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
       ON h3.instId = h2.instId AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
     WHERE h2.instId = l.instId
     AND h2.rn <= 30) AS atr_slow
FROM v_ticks_latest l
v_hist_ordered|CREATE VIEW v_hist_ordered AS
SELECT
    h.instId,
    h.lastPr,
    h.ts_ms,
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
        PARTITION BY h.instId
        ORDER BY h.ts_ms DESC
    ) AS rn
FROM ticks_hist h
v_momentum_1|CREATE VIEW v_momentum_1 AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    (l.lastPr - h.lastPr) AS momentum_1,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_hist_ordered h
    ON h.instId = l.instId AND h.rn = 1
v_momentum_acc|CREATE VIEW v_momentum_acc AS
SELECT
    m.instId,
    m.ts_ms,
    (
        SELECT SUM(h2.lastPr - h3.lastPr)
        FROM v_hist_ordered h2
        JOIN v_hist_ordered h3
            ON h3.instId = h2.instId
           AND h3.rn = h2.rn + 1
        WHERE h2.instId = m.instId
        AND h2.rn <= 10
    ) AS momentum_acc
FROM v_momentum_1 m
v_tick_classifier|CREATE VIEW v_tick_classifier AS
SELECT
    a.instId,
    CASE
        WHEN a.atr_fast IS NULL THEN 'NEUTRAL'
        WHEN a.atr_fast > a.atr_slow * 1.8 THEN 'BREAKOUT'
        WHEN a.atr_fast < a.atr_slow * 0.4 THEN 'SQUEEZE'
        ELSE 'CHOP'
    END AS class_signal
FROM v_atr a
v_tick_range|CREATE VIEW v_tick_range AS
SELECT instId,
       ABS(lastPr - prevPr) AS tr,
       ts_ms
FROM v_hist_ordered
WHERE prevPr IS NOT NULL
v_tick_range_position|CREATE VIEW v_tick_range_position AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT instId,lastPr,ts_ms,
           ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms DESC) rn
    FROM ticks_hist
),
range_win AS (
    SELECT instId,lastPr FROM base WHERE rn <= 26
),
agg AS (
    SELECT instId, MIN(lastPr) AS minP, MAX(lastPr) AS maxP
    FROM range_win GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT
   t.instId,
   t.lastPr,
   t.ts_ms,
   CASE WHEN a.maxP = a.minP THEN 0.5
        ELSE (t.lastPr - a.minP)/(a.maxP - a.minP)
   END AS pos_in_range
FROM ticks t
JOIN agg a USING(instId)
v_tick_volatility|CREATE VIEW v_tick_volatility AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        ts_ms,
        ABS(lastPr - LAG(lastPr) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms)) AS tr,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_ms DESC) AS rn
    FROM ticks_hist
)
SELECT
    instId,
    AVG(CASE WHEN rn <= 11 THEN tr END) AS atr_fast,
    AVG(CASE WHEN rn <= 26 THEN tr END) AS atr_slow
FROM base
GROUP BY instId
v_ticks_for_follower|CREATE VIEW v_ticks_for_follower AS
SELECT
    l.instId,
    l.lastPr,
    m1.momentum_1,
    COALESCE(macc.momentum_acc, 0) AS momentum_acc,
    a.atr_fast,
    a.atr_slow,
    0 AS pos_in_range,           -- volontairement ignoré (non utilisé)
    c.class_signal,
    l.ts_ms
FROM v_ticks_latest l
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_1 m1 ON m1.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_momentum_acc macc ON macc.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_atr a ON a.instId = l.instId
LEFT JOIN v_tick_classifier c ON c.instId = l.instId
v_ticks_latest|CREATE VIEW v_ticks_latest AS
SELECT
    t.instId,
    t.lastPr,
    t.ts_ms
FROM ticks t

-- INDEXES --
idx_hist_inst_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_hist_inst_ts ON ticks_hist(instId, ts_ms DESC)
sqlite_autoindex_ticks_1|

-- VIEWS --
v_trigger|CREATE VIEW v_trigger AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId_raw AS instId,
    side,
    type_signal,
    strength,
    confluence,
    ts_signal,
    status
FROM trigger_signals
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
v_wticks_tasks|CREATE VIEW v_wticks_tasks AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    ts_signal,
    price_signal,
    status
FROM wticks_tasks
v_wticks_window|CREATE VIEW v_wticks_window AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,

    MIN(CASE WHEN window_phase='pre'  THEN ts_tick END) AS first_pre_ts,
    MAX(CASE WHEN window_phase='pre'  THEN ts_tick END) AS last_pre_ts,
    MIN(CASE WHEN window_phase='post' THEN ts_tick END) AS first_post_ts,
    MAX(CASE WHEN window_phase='post' THEN ts_tick END) AS last_post_ts,

    MAX(CASE WHEN window_phase='post' THEN price END) AS post_peak_price,
    MIN(CASE WHEN window_phase='pre'  THEN price END) AS pre_valley_price

FROM wticks_data
GROUP BY uid, instId

-- INDEXES --
idx_wticks_inst|CREATE INDEX idx_wticks_inst ON wticks_data(instId)
idx_wticks_uid|CREATE INDEX idx_wticks_uid  ON wticks_data(uid)
sqlite_autoindex_trigger_1|
sqlite_autoindex_trigger_signals_1|
sqlite_autoindex_wticks_data_1|
sqlite_autoindex_wticks_tasks_1|

----- DATABASE: /opt/scalp/project/data/triggers.db -----
-- TABLES --
trig_state         triggers           v_triggers_latest

[TABLE: trig_state]
0|instId|TEXT|0||1
1|reason|TEXT|0||0
2|side|TEXT|0||0
3|score|REAL|0||0
4|ts|INTEGER|0||0

[TABLE: triggers]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|instId|TEXT|1||0
2|tf|TEXT|1||0
3|side|TEXT|1||0
4|reason|TEXT|1||0
5|score|REAL|1|0|0
6|ctx|TEXT|0||0
7|confidence|REAL|1|0|0
8|price|REAL|0||0
9|atr|REAL|0||0
10|ts|INTEGER|1||0
11|consumed|INTEGER|0|0|0

[TABLE: v_triggers_latest]
0|instId|TEXT|0||0
1|side|TEXT|0||0
2|reason|TEXT|0||0
3|score_B|REAL|0||0
4|ctx|TEXT|0||0
5|price|REAL|0||0
6|atr|REAL|0||0
7|ts_trigger|INTEGER|0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_triggers_latest|CREATE VIEW v_triggers_latest AS
WITH last_ts AS (
    SELECT instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_last
    FROM triggers
    GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT
    t.instId,
    t.side,
    t.reason,
    t.score   AS score_B,
    t.ctx,
    t.price,
    t.atr,
    t.ts      AS ts_trigger
FROM triggers t
JOIN last_ts lt
  ON lt.instId = t.instId AND lt.ts_last = t.ts
ORDER BY t.ts DESC

-- INDEXES --
idx_trig_consumed|CREATE INDEX idx_trig_consumed ON triggers(consumed)
idx_trig_instId|CREATE INDEX idx_trig_instId   ON triggers(instId)
idx_trig_tf|CREATE INDEX idx_trig_tf       ON triggers(tf)
idx_trig_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_trig_ts       ON triggers(ts)
sqlite_autoindex_trig_state_1|

v_wticks|CREATE VIEW v_wticks AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId,
    ts_ms,
    bid,
    ask,
    last,
    volume,
    window_pos
FROM wticks
ORDER BY uid, ts_ms
v_wticks_extended|CREATE VIEW v_wticks_extended AS
SELECT
    uid,
    instId_raw,
    ts_signal,
    peak_ts,
    peak_price,
    delta_t_ms,
    delta_price_pct,
    window_min_price,
    window_max_price,
    window_mean_price,
    window_var_price,
    pressure_bias,
    ts_created,
    ts_updated
FROM wticks_extended
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
